Gur fnyr bs guvf obbx jvgubhg vgf pbire vf hanhgubevmrq. Vs lbh chepunfrq
guvf obbx jvgubhg n pbire, lbh fubhyq or njner gung vg jnf ercbegrq gb
gur choyvfure nf "hafbyq naq qrfgeblrq." Arvgure gur nhgube abe gur
choyvfure unf erprvirq cnlzrag sbe gur fnyr bs guvf "fgevccrq obbx."

Guvf obbx vf n jbex bs svpgvba. Anzrf, punenpgref, cynprf naq
vapvqragf ner rvgure cebqhpgf bs gur nhgube'f vzntvangvba be ner
hfrq svpgvgvbhfyl. Nal erfrzoynapr gb npghny riragf be ybpnyrf be
crefbaf, yvivat be qrnq, vf ragveryl pbvapvqragny.

VAGEBQHPGVBA

Xyvatba vf gur bssvpvny ynathntr bs gur Xyvatba Rzcver. Sbe n
ybat gvzr, bayl n srj aba-Xyvatbaf jrer noyr gb yrnea rabhtu
nobhg gur ynathntr gb ratntr va n zrnavatshy pbairefngvba
jvgu n Xyvatba. Erpragyl, ubjrire, haqre gur nhfcvprf bs gur
Srqrengvba Fpvragvsvp Erfrnepu Pbhapvy, n fghql unf orra
haqregnxra gb erpbeq naq nanylmr gur ynathntr naq phygher bs
gur Xyvatbaf, jvgu gur hygvzngr tbny bs cercnevat na raplpyb-
crqvn, nf jryy nf grnpuvat zngrevnyf. Guvf qvpgvbanel ercer-
fragf gur vavgvny erfhygf bs gung rssbeg.
  Gur qvpgvbanel vf qvivqrq vagb gjb znva cnegf: tenzzngvpny
fxrgpu naq qvpgvbanel cebcre.
  Gur tenzzngvpny fxrgpu vf vagraqrq gb or na bhgyvar bs
Xyvatba tenzzne, abg n pbzcyrgr qrfpevcgvba. Arireguryrff,
vg fubhyq nyybj gur ernqre gb chg Xyvatba jbeqf gbtrgure va na
npprcgnoyr znaare. Znal bs gur ehyrf tvira va gur tenzzngv-
pny fxrgpu ner gubfr frg qbja ol Xyvatba tenzznevnaf. Vg
fubhyq or erzrzorerq gung rira gubhtu gur ehyrf fnl "ny-
jnlf" naq "arire," jura Xyvatba vf npghnyyl fcbxra gurfr
ehyrf ner fbzrgvzrf oebxra. Jung gur ehyrf ercerfrag, va
bgure jbeqf, vf jung Xyvatba tenzznevnaf nterr ba nf gur
"orfg" Xyvatba.
  Orpnhfr erfrnepu vf abg lrg pbzcyrgrq, guvf qvpgvbanel vf bs
arprffvgl fbzrjung yvzvgrq va fpbcr. Gurer ner pregnvayl
zber Xyvatba jbeqf guna gubfr yvfgrq urer. Guerr tebhcf bs [[c.10]]
jbeqf va cnegvphyne ner, sbe gur zbfg cneg, haercerfragrq:
fpvragvsvp grezvabybtl; jbeqf sbe angvir gbbyf, phfgbzf, syben,
naq snhan; naq ibpnohynel qrnyvat jvgu sbbq. Grezf nffbpvng-
rq jvgu gur inevbhf fpvraprf ner gur fhowrpg bs n fcrpvny fghql,
naq n ercbeg vf pheeragyl orvat cercnerq. Xyvatba jbeqf sbe
genqvgvbany gbbyf naq ybat-fgnaqvat phfgbzf ner qvssvphyg gb
genafyngr vagb Ratyvfu. Angvir cynagf naq navznyf ner yvxrjvfr
qvssvphyg gb pbzceruraq ng gur cerfrag gvzr. Fhpu znggref jvyy
or shyyl ryhpvqngrq va gur sbegupbzvat <Xyvatba Raplpybcrqvn.>
Sbbq jbeqf ner zvffvat qhr gb yvzvgrq erfbheprf: gurer unir
orra ceboyrzf erpehvgvat fgnss vagrerfgrq va fghqlvat Xyvatba
rngvat unovgf. Hagvy gung fghql vf haqre jnl, vg jnf gubhtug
vanccebcevngr gb cerfrag n yvfg bs jbeqf jubfr zrnavatf ner
abg cebcreyl haqrefgbbq.
  Nf zber qngn ner tngurerq gur yvfg bs jbeqf jvyy haqbhogrq-
yl tebj. Rira ng guvf rneyl fgntr, ubjrire, fbzr cnggreaf ner
rzretvat. Sbe rknzcyr, gurer ner ab jbeqf sbe terrgvatf,
fhpu nf <uryyb, ubj ner lbh, tbbq zbeavat,> naq fb ba. Vg frrzf
nccnerag gung fhpu jbeqf naq cuenfrf fvzcyl qb abg rkvfg va
Xyvatba. Jura gjb Xyvatbaf zrrg rnpu bgure (rkprcg va pnfrf
jurer zvyvgnel cebgbpby qrgrezvarf orunivbe), vs nalguvat bs
na vagebqhpgbel angher vf fnvq, vg vf na rkcerffvba gung pna orfg
or genafyngrq nf <Jung qb lbh jnag?> Hayvxr zbfg fcrnxref bs
Ratyvfu, jub ortva pbairefngvbaf jvgu terrgvatf, vadhvevrf
nobhg gur fgngr bs urnygu bs gur pbairefnagf, naq erznexf
nobhg gur jrngure, Xyvatbaf graq gb ortva pbairefngvbaf ol
fvzcyl fgngvat gur znva cbvagf.
  Nygubhtu Xyvatbaf ner cebhq bs gurve ynathntr naq ser-
dhragyl ratntr va ybat qvfphffvbaf nobhg vgf rkcerffvirarff
naq ornhgl, gurl unir sbhaq vg vzcenpgvpny sbe pbzzhavpngvba
bhgfvqr gur Xyvatba Rzcver. Sbe vagen- naq vagretnynpgvp
pbzzhavpngvba, gur Xyvatba tbireazrag, nybat jvgu zbfg
bgure tbireazragf, unf npprcgrq Ratyvfu nf gur yvathn senapn.
Va trareny, bayl gubfr Xyvatbaf bs gur hccre pynffrf (juvpu
vapyhqr uvture-yriry tbireazragny naq zvyvgnel bssvpvnyf) yrnea
Ratyvfu. Nf n erfhyg, Ratyvfu unf gnxra ba gjb nqqvgvbany
shapgvbaf va Xyvatba fbpvrgl. Svefg, vg vf hfrq nf n flzoby bs
enax be fgnghf. Gubfr Xyvatbaf jub xabj Ratyvfu jvyy hfr vg
nzbat gurzfryirf gb fubj bss gurve rehqvgvba naq znxr gurve
cynpr va fbpvrgl xabja gb nyy jub unccra gb or yvfgravat.
Frpbaq, Ratyvfu vf hfrq jura vg vf gubhtug orfg gb xrrc [[c.11]]
freinagf, fbyqvref, be rira gur trareny cbchynpr havasbezrq.
Guhf, ba n Xyvatba irffry, gur pbzznaqvat bssvpre jvyy bsgra
fcrnx Xyvatba jura tvivat beqref gb uvf perj, ohg pubbfr
Ratyvfu jura univat qvfphffvbaf jvgu uvf bssvpref. Ba gur
bgure unaq, n Xyvatba bssvpre znl hfr Xyvatba va gur cerfrapr
bs aba-Xyvatbaf gb cerirag gurz sebz xabjvat jung vf tbvat
ba. Guvf hfr bs Xyvatba frrzf gb or dhvgr rssrpgvir.
  Gurer ner n ahzore bs qvnyrpgf bs Xyvatba. Bayl bar bs gur
qvnyrpgf, gung bs gur pheerag Xyvatba rzcrebe, vf ercerfragrq
va guvf qvpgvbanel. Jura n Xyvatba rzcrebe vf ercynprq, sbe
jungrire ernfba, vg unf uvfgbevpnyyl orra gur pnfr gung gur arkg
rzcrebe fcrnxf n qvssrerag qvnyrpg. Nf n erfhyg, gur arj
rzcrebe'f qvnyrpg orpbzrf gur bssvpvny qvnyrpg. Gubfr Xyvat-
baf jub qb abg fcrnx gur bssvpvny qvnyrpg ner pbafvqrerq
rvgure fghcvq be fhoirefvir, naq ner hfhnyyl sbeprq gb haqregnxr
gnfxf gung fcrnxref bs gur bssvpvny qvnyrpg svaq qvfgnfgrshy. Zbfg
Xyvatbaf gel gb or syhrag va frireny qvnyrpgf.
  Fbzr qvnyrpgf qvssre bayl fyvtugyl sebz gur qvnyrpg bs guvf
qvpgvbanel. Qvssreraprf graq gb or va ibpnohynel (gur jbeq sbe
<sberurnq,> sbe rknzcyr, vf qvssrerag va nyzbfg rirel qvnyrpg)
naq va gur cebahapvngvba bs n srj fbhaqf. Ba gur bgure unaq,
fbzr qvnyrpgf qvssre fvtavsvpnagyl sebz gur pheerag bssvpvny
qvnyrpg, fb zhpu fb gung fcrnxref bs gurfr qvnyrpgf unir n terng
qrny bs qvssvphygl pbzzhavpngvat jvgu pheerag Xyvatba bssvpvny-
qbz. Gur fghqrag bs Xyvatba vf jnearq gb purpx vagb gur
cbyvgvpny fvghngvba bs gur Xyvatba Rzcver orsber gelvat gb
gnyx.
  Gurer vf n angvir jevgvat flfgrz sbe Xyvatba (pnyyrq {cVdnQ})
juvpu frrzf gb or jryy fhvgrq gb gur inevbhf qvnyrpgf. Guvf
jevgvat flfgrz vf abg lrg jryy haqrefgbbq naq vf, gurersber,
abg hfrq va guvf qvpgvbanel. Vafgrnq, n genafpevcgvba flfgrz
onfrq ba gur Ratyvfu nycunorg unf orra qrivfrq. Na negvpyr vf
orvat cercnerq sbe gur <Xyvatba Raplpybcrqvn> juvpu jvyy
rkcynva gur qrgnvyf bs {cVdnQ.}
  Va gur tenzzngvpny fxrgpu cbegvba bs guvf qvpgvbanel, nf n
abgngvbany pbairagvba, Xyvatba jvyy or jevggra va obyqsnpr
glcr, naq Ratyvfu genafyngvbaf jvyy or jevggra va vgnyvpf:
{gyuVatna} <Xyvatba.>
  Gur nhgube jbhyq yvxr gb gunax gur Fpvragvsvp Erfrnepu
Pbhapvy sbe znxvat shaqf ninvynoyr gb pneel bhg guvf erfrnepu,
nf jryy nf inevbhf zrzoref bs gur Srqrengvba Vagreynathntr [[c.12]]
Vafgvghgr jub jrer dhvgr urycshy va pevgvpvmvat rneyvre qensgf bs
gur qvpgvbanel. Gur nhgube ncbybtvmrf sbe nal zvfgnxrf, naq
fvapreryl ubcrf gung abar bs gurz yrnqf gb nal hasbeghangr
zvfhaqrefgnaqvatf.
  Svanyyl, n terng qrny bs perqvg zhfg or tvira gb gur Xyvatba
vasbeznag jub cebivqrq nyy bs gur qngn hcba juvpu guvf
qvpgvbanel vf onfrq. Nygubhtu n cevfbare bs gur Srqrengvba, ur
jbexrq ybat, uneq ubhef gb znxr uvf xabjyrqtr ninvynoyr gb
pvgvmraf bs gur Srqrengvba. Znygm, jr gunax lbh. [[c.13]]


1. GUR FBHAQF BS XYVATBA

Vg vf qvssvphyg gb qrfpevor npphengryl gur fbhaqf bs gur Xyvatba
ynathntr jvgubhg hfvat pbzcyrk cubabybtvpny naq nangbzvpny
grezvabybtl. Jung sbyybjf, gurersber, vf vagraqrq gb tvir bayl
n thvqr gb cebahapvngvba. Gur orfg jnl gb yrnea gb cebabhapr
Xyvatba jvgu ab genpr bs n Greena be bgure npprag vf gb orpbzr
sevraqf jvgu n tebhc bs Xyvatbaf naq fcraq n terng qrny bs
gvzr fbpvnyvmvat jvgu gurz. Irel srj aba-Xyvatbaf fcrnx
Xyvatba jvgubhg na npprag.
  Gur flfgrz bs jevgvat Xyvatba hfrq va guvf qvpgvbanel unf
orra qrirybcrq fb crbcyr jub nyernql xabj ubj gb ernq
Ratyvfu jvyy unir n zvavzhz bs qvssvphygl nccebkvzngvat gur
fbhaqf bs Xyvatba jbeqf naq fragraprf.


1.1. Pbafbanagf

  {o} Nf va Ratyvfu <oebapuvgvf> be <tnmrob.> Fbzr Xyvatbaf
cebabhapr guvf fbhaq nf vs vg jrer {z} naq {o} negvphyngrq nyzbfg
fvzhygnarbhfyl. Fcrnxref bs Ratyvfu pna nccebkvzngr
guvf fbhaq ol fnlvat <vzonynapr> jvgubhg gur vavgvny <v> fbhaq.
N irel fznyy ahzore bs Xyvatbaf cebabhapr {o} nf vs vg jrer {z.}
  {pu} Nf va Ratyvfu <purj> be <negvpubxr.>
  {Q} Guvf fbhaq vf pybfr gb Ratyvfu <q> va <qernz> be <naqebvq,> ohg
vg vf abg dhvgr gur fnzr. Gur Ratyvfu <q> fbhaq vf znqr ol [[c.14]]
gbhpuvat gur gvc bs gur gbathr gb gung cneg bs gur ebbs bs gur
zbhgu whfg oruvaq gur hccre grrgu. Xyvatba {Q} pna orfg or
nccebkvzngrq ol Ratyvfu-fcrnxref ol gbhpuvat gur gvc bs gur
gbathr gb gur ebbs bs gur zbhgu ng n cbvag nobhg unysjnl
orgjrra gur grrgu naq gur iryhz (be fbsg cnyngr), gung cneg bs
gur ebbs bs gur zbhgu gung vf engure tbbful. Nf jvgu Xyvatba
{o,} fbzr fcrnxref cebabhapr {Q} nf vs vg jrer zber yvxr <aq,> naq
n qvfgvapg zvabevgl nf vs vg jrer {a}---ohg, bs pbhefr, jvgu gur
gbathr va gur fnzr cbfvgvba nf sbe {Q.}
  {tu} Guvf vf abg yvxr nalguvat va Ratyvfu. Vg pna or cebqhprq
ol chggvat gur gbathr va gur fnzr cbfvgvba vg jbhyq or va gb
fnl Ratyvfu <t> nf va <tbooyr,> ohg erynkvat gur gbathr fbzrjung
naq uhzzvat. Vg vf gur fnzr nf Xyvatba {U} (frr orybj), ohg
jvgu gur ibpny pbeqf ivoengvat ng gur fnzr gvzr.
  {U} Guvf vf nyfb abg yvxr nalguvat va Ratyvfu, ohg vg vf whfg yvxr
<pu> va gur anzr bs gur Trezna pbzcbfre <Onpu> be va gur
Lvqqvfu gbnfg <y'punvz,> be gur <w> va gur Zrkvpna pvgl bs <Gvwhnan>
va <Onwn Pnyvsbeavn.> Vg vf cebqhprq va gur fnzr jnl nf Xyvatba
{tu,} ohg vf negvphyngrq jvgu n irel pbnefr, fgebat enfc. Hayvxr
Xyvatba {tu,} gur ibpny pbeqf qb abg ivoengr va fnlvat Xyvatba
{U.}
  {w} Nf va Ratyvfu <whax;> arire rire nf va Serapu <wbhe.>
  {y} Nf va Ratyvfu <yhatr> be <nypurzl.>
  {z} Nf va Ratyvfu <zhq> be <carhzngvp.> Gubfr srj Xyvatbaf
jub cebabhapr {o} nf {z} jbhyq fnl Xyvatba {onU} <sver (n gbecrqb)>
naq {znU} <jr> gur fnzr jnl, naq unir gb zrzbevmr juvpu jbeq
vf fcryyrq juvpu jnl.
  {a} Nf va Ratyvfu <arpgnevar> be <fhafcbg.> Gubfr Xyvatbaf jub
cebabhapr {Q} zber yvxr {a} pna rnfvyl negvphyngr naq urne gur
gjb fbhaqf qvssreragyl. Rira n {Q} gung fbhaqf yvxr {a} vf
cebabhaprq jvgu gur gbathr va gur Xyvatba {Q} cbfvgvba, abg va
gur Ratyvfu <q> cbfvgvba. Xyvatba {a} vf cebqhprq jvgu gur gbathr
va gur fnzr cbfvgvba nf Ratyvfu <q.>
  {at} Nf va Ratyvfu <sheybat;> arire nf va Ratyvfu <rathys.> Gur <t>
vf arire cebabhaprq nf n frcnengr fbhaq. Guvf fbhaq arire
bpphef ng gur ortvaavat bs na Ratyvfu jbeq, ohg vg qbrf pbzr
ng gur ortvaavat bs n ahzore bs Xyvatba jbeqf. Ratyvfu- [[xrrc ulcura]]
fcrnxref znl cenpgvpr znxvat guvf fbhaq ng gur ortvaavat bs n
jbeq ol fnlvat Ratyvfu <qnat vg!,> gura fnlvat vg ntnva jvgubhg
gur <qn.>
  {c} Nf va Ratyvfu <cnenyynk> be <bcceboevhz.> Vg vf nyjnlf [[c.15]]
negvphyngrq jvgu n fgebat chss be cbc, arire ynkyl. Fcrnxref bs
Ratyvfu znl jnag gb rkrepvfr pner gb nibvq qvfpunetvat fnyvin
juvyr negvphyngvat guvf fbhaq. Vg fubhyq or abgrq, ubjrire,
gung Xyvatbaf qb abg jbeel nobhg guvf.
  {d} Fvzvyne gb Ratyvfu <x> va <xhzdhng,> ohg abg dhvgr gung. Gur
gbathr cbfvgvba sbe Ratyvfu <x> vf yvxr gung sbe Xyvatba {tu} naq
{U.} Gb cebqhpr Xyvatba {d,} gur znva obql bs gur gbathr
gbhpurf gur ebbs bs gur zbhgu ng n cbvag snegure onpx guna vg
qbrf sbe {tu} be {U.} Vaqrrq, gur gbathr ernpurf sbe be gbhpurf
gur hihyn (gur zrful oybo gung qnatyrf qbja sebz gur onpx bs
gur ebbs bs gur zbhgu), fb negvphyngvat {d} nccebkvzngrf gur
fbhaq bs pubxvat. Gur fbhaq vf hfhnyyl nppbzcnavrq ol n
fyvtug chss bs nve. Ratyvfu fcrnxref ner erzvaqrq gung Xyvatba
{d} vf arire cebabhaprq <xj> nf va gur ortvaavat bs Ratyvfu
<dhntzver.>
  {D} Guvf vf yvxr abguvat cnegvphyneyl abgrjbegul va Ratyvfu.
Vg vf na bireqbar Xyvatba {d.} Vg vf vqragvpny gb {d} rkprcg gung vg vf
irel thggheny naq enfcl naq fgebatyl negvphyngrq, fbzrjung
yvxr n oyraq bs Xyvatba {d} naq {U.}
  {e} Guvf vf abg yvxr gur <e> va Nzrevpna Ratyvfu, ohg vg qbrf
erfrzoyr gur <e> va fbzr qvnyrpgf bs Oevgvfu Ratyvfu, nf jryy nf
gur <e> va znal ynathntrf bs Rhebcr. Vg vf yvtugyl gevyyrq be
ebyyrq.
  {F} Guvf fbhaq vf unysjnl orgjrra Ratyvfu <f> naq <fu,> nf va
<flevatr> naq <fuhggyrpbpx.> Vg vf znqr jvgu gur gvc bs gur gbathr
ernpuvat gbjneq gung cneg bs gur ebbs bs gur zbhgu juvpu vg
gbhpurf gb cebqhpr Xyvatba {Q.}
  {g} Nf va Ratyvfu <gnecnhyva> be <pevgvdhr.> Vg qvssref sebz Xyvat-
ba {Q} va gjb jnlf: (1) yvxr {c,} vg vf nppbzcnavrq ol n chss bs nve;
naq (2) gur gbathr gbhpurf n cbfvgvba ba gur ebbs bs gur
zbhgu snegure sbejneq guna gung sbe {Q.}
  {gyu} Guvf fbhaq qbrf abg bpphe va Ratyvfu, ohg vg vf irel
zhpu yvxr gur svany fbhaq va <grgy,> gur Nmgrp jbeq sbe <rtt,> vs
cebcreyl cebabhaprq. Gb cebqhpr guvf fbhaq, gur gvc bs gur
gbathr gbhpurf gur fnzr cneg bs gur ebbs bs gur zbhgu vg
gbhpurf sbe {g,} gur fvqrf bs gur gbathr ner ybjrerq njnl sebz
gur fvqr hccre grrgu, naq nve vf sbeprq guebhtu gur fcnpr ba
obgu fvqrf orgjrra gbathr naq grrgu. Gur fbhaq vf cebqhprq
jvgu n terng qrny bs sevpgvba, naq gur jneavat tvira va gur
qrfpevcgvba bs Xyvatba {c} zvtug or ncgyl ercrngrq urer.
  {i} Nf va Ratyvfu <ihytne> be <qrzbafgengvir>. [[c.16]]
  {j} Hfhnyyl nf va Ratyvfu <jbeeljneg> be <pbj.> Ba ener bppn-
fvbaf, rfcrpvnyyl vs gur fcrnxre vf orvat engure qryvorengr, vg vf
cebabhaprq fgebatyl, zber yvxr {Uj} be rira {Uhj.}
  {l} Nf va Ratyvfu <lbqry> be <wbl.>
  {'} Gur ncbfgebcur vaqvpngrf n fbhaq juvpu vf serdhragyl
hggrerq, ohg abg jevggra, va Ratyvfu. Vg vf n tybggny fgbc, gur
fyvtug pngpu va gur guebng orgjrra gur gjb flyynoyrf bs <hu-bu> be
<hau-hau,> zrnavat "ab." Jura Xyvatba {'} pbzrf ng gur raq bs
n jbeq, gur ibjry cerprqvat gur {'} vf bsgra ercrngrq va n irel
fbsg juvfcre, nf vs na rpub. Guhf, Xyvatba {wr'} <srrq> nyzbfg
fbhaqf yvxr {wr'r,} jurer gur negvphyngvba bs gur svefg {r} vf
noehcgyl phg bss ol gur {',} naq gur frpbaq {r} vf n oneryl nhqvoyr
juvfcre. Jura {'} sbyybjf {j} be {l} ng gur raq bs n jbeq, gurer vf
bsgra n juvfcrerq, rpubrq {h} be {V,} erfcrpgviryl. Bppnfvbanyyl
gur rpub vf dhvgr nhqvoyr, jvgu n thggheny fbhaq yvxr {tu}
cerprqvat gur rpubrq ibjry. Sbe rknzcyr, {lVyV'} <genafzvg
vg!> pna fbhaq zber yvxr {lVyV'tuV.} Guvf rkgen-urnil rpub vf
urneq zbfg bsgra jura gur fcrnxre vf cnegvphyneyl rkpvgrq be
natel.


1.2. Ibjryf

Gurer ner svir ibjryf va Xyvatba.

  {n} Nf va Ratyvfu <cfnyz;> arire nf va Nzrevpna Ratyvfu
<penonccyr.>
  {r} Nf va Ratyvfu <frafbe.>
  {V} Nf Ratyvfu <v> va <zvfsvg.> Bapr va n juvyr, vg vf cebabhaprq
yvxr <v> va <mhppuvav,> ohg guvf vf irel ener naq vg vf abg lrg xabja
rknpgyl jung pvephzfgnaprf nppbhag sbe vg,
  {b} Nf va Ratyvfu <zbfnvp.>
  {h} Nf va Ratyvfu <tah> be <cehar;> arire nf va <ohg> be <phgr.>

  Abgr gung jura n ibjry vf sbyybjrq ol {j} be {l,} gur
pbzovangvba bs yrggref znl abg ercerfrag gur fnzr fbhaq vg
qbrf va Ratyvfu fcryyvat:

  XYVATBA  EULZRF JVGU RATYVFU  NF VA
    {nj}           <bj>           <pbj>
    {nl}           <l>            <pel>
    {rl}           <nl>           <cnl> [[c.17]]
    {Vl}           <rl>           <xrl>
    {bl}           <bl>           <gbl>

  Xyvatba {hl} erfrzoyrf <bbrl> va Ratyvfu <tbbrl.> Xyvatba {rj}
erfrzoyrf abguvat va Ratyvfu, ohg pna or nccebkvzngrq ol
ehaavat Xyvatba {r} naq {h} gbtrgure. Yvxrjvfr, Xyvatba {Vj} vf {V}
naq {h} eha gbtrgure. Ab jbeqf va Xyvatba unir {bj} be {hj.} Vs
gurl qvq, gurl jbhyq or vaqvfgvathvfunoyr sebz jbeqf raqvat
va {b} naq {h,} erfcrpgviryl.


1.3. Fgerff

Rnpu Xyvatba jbeq bs zber guna bar flyynoyr abeznyyl
pbagnvaf bar fgerffrq (be nppragrq) flyynoyr. Gur fgerffrq
flyynoyr vf cebabhaprq ng n fyvtugyl uvture cvgpu naq jvgu n
yvggyr zber sbepr guna gur abafgerffrq flyynoyr(f).
  Va n ireo, gur fgerffrq flyynoyr vf hfhnyyl gur ireo vgfrys, nf
bccbfrq gb nal cersvk be fhssvk. Vs, ubjrire, n fhssvk raqvat
jvgu {'} vf frcnengrq sebz gur ireo ol ng yrnfg bar bgure fhssvk,
obgu gur ireo naq gur fhssvk raqvat va {'} ner fgerffrq. Va
nqqvgvba, vs gur zrnavat bs nal cnegvphyne fhssvk vf gb or
rzcunfvmrq, gur fgerff znl fuvsg gb gung flyynoyr. Fhssvkrf
vaqvpngvat artngvba be rzcunfvf (frpgvba 4.3) ner serdhragyl
fgerffrq, nf vf gur vagreebtngvir fhssvk (frpgvba 4.2.9).
  Va n abha, gur fgerffrq flyynoyr vf hfhnyyl gur flyynoyr evtug
orsber gur svefg abha fhssvk, be gur svany flyynoyr vs gurer vf ab
fhssvk. Vs, ubjrire, n flyynoyr raqvat va {'} vf cerfrag, vg vf
hfhnyyl fgerffrq vafgrnq. Vs gurer ner gjb flyynoyrf va n ebj
{'} obgu raqvat va {',} obgu ner rdhnyyl fgerffrq.
  Svanyyl, vg fubhyq or abgrq gung gurer ner fbzr jbeqf juvpu
frrz gb unir inevnoyr fgerff cnggreaf, jvgu gur fgerff fbzr-
gvzrf urneq ba bar flyynoyr naq fbzrgvzrf ba nabgure. Guvf
curabzraba vf abg lrg haqrefgbbq. Gur ehyrf tvira nobir qb
abg nppbhag sbe guvf inevnovyvgl, ohg vs gurl ner sbyybjrq, fgerff
jvyy jvaq hc ba npprcgnoyr flyynoyrf.
  Va gur flfgrz hfrq gb genafpevor Xyvatba va guvf qvpgvbanel,
fgerff vf abg vaqvpngrq. [[c.18]]


2. TENZZNGVPNY FXRGPU---VAGEBQHPGVBA

Vg vf abg cbffvoyr, va n oevrs thvqr fhpu nf guvf, gb qrfpevor gur
tenzzne bs Xyvatba pbzcyrgryl. Jung sbyybjf vf bayl n
fxrgpu be bhgyvar bs Xyvatba tenzzne. Nygubhtu n tbbq znal
bs gur svar cbvagf ner abg pbirerq, gur fxrgpu jvyy nyybj gur
fghqrag bs Xyvatba gb svther bhg jung n Xyvatba vf fnlvat naq
gb erfcbaq va na vagryyvtvoyr, gubhtu fbzrjung oehgvfu,
znaare. Zbfg Xyvatbaf jvyy arire xabj gur qvssrerapr.

  Gurer ner guerr onfvp cnegf bs fcrrpu va Xyvatba: <abha,
ireo,> naq <rirelguvat ryfr.> [[c.19]]


3. ABHAF

Gurer ner inevbhf glcrf bs abhaf va Xyvatba.


3.1. Fvzcyr abhaf

Fvzcyr abhaf, yvxr fvzcyr abhaf va Ratyvfu, ner fvzcyr jbeqf;
sbe rknzcyr, {QbF} <gnetrg> be {DVU} <qrfgehpgvba.>


3.2. Pbzcyrk abhaf

Pbzcyrk abhaf, ba gur bgure unaq, ner znqr hc bs zber guna
bar cneg.


3.2.1. Pbzcbhaq abhaf

Pbzcbhaq abhaf pbafvfg bs gjb be guerr abhaf va n ebj,
zhpu yvxr Ratyvfu <rnegujbez> (<rnegu> cyhf <jbez>) be <cnffjbeq>
(<cnff> cyhf <jbeq>). Sbe rknzcyr, {wbycn'} <genafcbegebbz> pbafvfgf
bs {wby} <genafcbeg ornz> cyhf {cn'} <ebbz.>


3.2.2. Ireo cyhf -jV'

N frpbaq glcr bs pbzcyrk abha pbafvfgf bs n ireo sbyybjrq ol
n fhssvk zrnavat <bar jub qbrf> be <guvat juvpu qbrf>. Gur
Ratyvfu fhssvk <-re> (nf va <ohvyqre> "bar jub ohvyqf" be <gbnfgre>
"guvat juvpu gbnfgf") vf n ebhtu rdhvinyrag. Va Xyvatba, gur [[c.20]]
fhssvk vf {-jV'.} Vg bpphef, sbe rknzcyr, va {onUjV'} <thaare,> juvpu
pbafvfgf bs gur ireo {onU} <sver (n gbecrqb)> cyhf {-jV'} <bar jub
qbrf.> Guhf, {onUjV'} vf yvgrenyyl "bar jub sverf [n gbecrqb]."
Fvzvyneyl, {Fb'jV'} <pybnxvat qrivpr> pbzrf sebz gur ireo {Fb'}
<pybnx> cyhf {-jV'} <guvat juvpu qbrf.> {Fb'jV'} vf n "guvat juvpu
pybnxf."

N abha sbezrq ol nqqvat {-jV'} gb n ireo vf n erthyne abha,
fb vg znl or hfrq nybat jvgu nabgure abha gb sbez n
pbzcbhaq abha. Sbe rknzcyr, {gVwjV'tubz} <obneqvat cnegl>
pbzrf sebz {gVwjV'} <obneqre> cyhf {tubz} <tebhc;> naq {gVwjV'} pbzrf
sebz {gVw} <obneq> cyhf {-jV'.}


3.2.3. Bgure pbzcyrk abhaf

Gurer ner n tbbq znal abhaf va Xyvatba juvpu ner gjb be,
yrff serdhragyl, guerr flyynoyrf ybat, ohg juvpu ner abg
pbzcyrk abhaf bs gur glcrf qrfpevorq nobir. Gurfr abhaf
cebonoyl ng bar gvzr jrer sbezrq ol pbzovavat fvzcyr
abhaf, ohg bar be nyy bs gur abhaf sbezvat gur pbzcyrk abha
ner ab ybatre va hfr, fb vg vf abg cbffvoyr (jvgubhg rkgrafvir
rglzbybtvpny erfrnepu) gb xabj jung gur vaqvivqhny cvrprf
zrna.
  Sbe rknzcyr, {'rwQb'} zrnaf <fgnefuvc.> Gur flyynoyr {'rw} nyfb
bpphef va {'rwlb'} <Fgnesyrrg.> Gurer ner, ubjrire, ab xabja
Xyvatba jbeqf {'rw, Qb',} be {lb'} gung unir nalguvat gb qb jvgu
Fgnesyrrg, fgnefuvcf, gur Srqrengvba, be fcnpr iruvpyrf bs nal
xvaq. Vg vf dhvgr yvxryl gung {Qb'} vf na Byq Xyvatba jbeq sbe
fcnpr irffry (gur zbqrea Xyvatba jbeq vf {Qhw}) gung vf hfrq
abjurer rkprcg va gur abha {'rwQb'.} Bs pbhefr, jvgubhg
shegure fghql, gung erznvaf cher pbawrpgher.


3.3. Fhssvkrf [[Fhssvkrf:=Abha fhssvkrf]]

Nyy abhaf, jurgure fvzcyr be pbzcyrk, znl or sbyybjrq ol
bar be zber fhssvkrf. Vs gurer ner gjb be zber fhssvkrf, gur
fhssvkrf zhfg bpphe va n fcrpvsvp beqre. Fhssvkrf znl or
pynffvsvrq ba gur onfvf bs gurve eryngvir beqre nsgre gur abha.
Gurer ner svir glcrf bs fhssvkrf (juvpu, sbe pbairavrapr, jvyy
or ahzorerq 1 guebhtu 5). Fhssvkrf bs Glcr 1 pbzr evtug nsgre
gur abha; fhssvkrf bs Glcr 2 pbzr nsgre gubfr bs Glcr 1;
fhssvkrf bs Glcr 5 pbzr ynfg. Guvf znl or vyyhfgengrq nf
sbyybjf: [[c.21]]

  ABHA--1--2--3--4--5

Bs pbhefr, vs ab fhssvk bs Glcr 1 vf hfrq ohg n fhssvk bs Glcr 2 vf
hfrq, gur Glcr 2 fhssvk pbzrf evtug nsgre gur abha. Vs n fhssvk
bs Glcr 5 vf gur bayl fhssvk hfrq, vg pbzrf evtug nsgre gur abha.
Bayl jura gjb be zber fhssvkrf ner hfrq qbrf gurve beqre
orpbzr nccnerag.
  Gurer ner ng yrnfg gjb fhssvkrf va rnpu fhssvk glcr. Bayl bar
fhssvk bs rnpu glcr znl or hfrq ng n gvzr. Gung vf, n abha
pnaabg or sbyybjrq ol, sbe rknzcyr, gjb be guerr Glcr 4
fhssvkrf.
  Gur zrzoref bs rnpu fhssvk glcr ner nf sbyybjf.


3.3.1. Glcr 1: Nhtzragngvir/qvzvahgvir

  {-'n'} <nhtzragngvir>

  Guvf fhssvk vaqvpngrf gung jung gur abha ersref gb vf ovttre,
zber vzcbegnag, be zber cbjreshy guna vg jbhyq or jvgubhg
gur fhssvk.

    {FhF} <jvaq, oerrmr>  {FhF'n'} <fgebat jvaq>
    {Dntu} <zvfgnxr>      {Dntu'n'} <znwbe oyhaqre>
    {jbD} <cbjre>         {jbD'n'} <hygvzngr cbjre>

  {-Ubz} <qvzvahgvir>

  Guvf vf gur bccbfvgr bs gur nhtzragngvir fhssvk. Vg vaqvpngrf
gung jung gur abha ersref gb vf fznyyre, yrff vzcbegnag, be yrff
cbjreshy guna vg jbhyq or jvgubhg gur fhssvk.

    {FhF} <jvaq, oerrmr>  {FhFUbz} <jvfc bs nve>
    {ebw} <crnpr>         {ebwUbz} <gehpr, grzcbenel crnpr>


3.3.2. Glcr 2: Ahzore

Nf va Ratyvfu, n fvathyne abha va Xyvatba unf ab fcrpvsvp fhssvk
vaqvpngvat gung vg vf fvathyne: {ahU} <jrncba> ersref gb n fvatyr
jrncba bs nal glcr. Hayvxr Ratyvfu, ubjrire, gur ynpx bs n
fcrpvsvp fhssvk sbe cyheny qbrf abg nyjnlf vaqvpngr gung gur abha
vf fvathyne. Va Xyvatba, n abha jvgubhg n cyheny fhssvk znl fgvyy
ersre gb zber guna bar ragvgl. Gur cyhenyvgl vf vaqvpngrq ol n [[c.22]]
cebabha, jurgure n ireo cersvk (frr frpgvba 4.1) be n shyy jbeq
(frpgvba 5.1), be ol pbagrkg. Sbe rknzcyr, {lnF} <bssvpre> znl
ersre gb n fvatyr bssvpre be gb n tebhc bs bssvpref, qrcraqvat ba
bgure jbeqf va gur fragrapr be gur pbagrkg bs gur qvfphffvba.
  Pbzcner:

    {lnF iVzbwch'} <V orpnzr na bssvpre.>
    {lnF QVzbwch'} <Jr orpnzr bssvpref.>

    {lnF wVU} <V nz na bssvpre.>
    {lnF znU} <Jr ner bssvpref.>

Va gur svefg cnve bs fragraprf, gur bayl qvssrerapr vf gur ireo
cersvk (urer bayl cnegvnyyl qrfpevorq; frr frpgvba 4.1): {iV-} <V,>
{QV-} <jr.> Va gur frpbaq cnve, gur cebabhaf ner qvssrerag: {wVU} <V,>
{znU} <jr.>
  Haqre pregnva pvephzfgnaprf, gur bayl jnl gb xabj jurgu-
re gur abha ersref gb bar be zber guna bar ragvgl vf ol
pbagrkg. Guhf, {lnF zbwch'} pna or genafyngrq rvgure <ur/fur
orpnzr na bssvpre> be <gurl orpnzr bssvpref.> Gubfr gnxvat cneg va
nal qvfphffvba va juvpu guvf fragrapr vf hfrq jbhyq cerfhz-
noyl nyernql xabj jubz vf orvat gnyxrq nobhg, fb gurl jbhyq
nyfb xabj jurgure ur be fur be gurl vf gur pbeerpg zrnavat.
  Sbeghangryl sbe fghqragf bs Xyvatba, vg vf arire vapbeerpg gb
nqq n cyheny fhssvk gb n abha ersreevat gb zber guna bar ragvgl,
rira va gubfr pnfrf jurer vg vf haarprffnel gb qb fb. Nppbeq-
vatyl, obgu {lnF znU} naq {lnFch' znU} ner pbeerpg, obgu
zrnavat <jr ner bssvpref> ({-ch'} vf n cyheny fhssvk). Ba gur bgure
unaq, n cyheny fhssvk pnaabg or nqqrq gb n abha ersreevat gb
bayl bar guvat, rira vs cebabhaf ner cerfrag va gur fragrapr.
Va Xyvatba, {lnFch' wVU} <V nz bssvpref> vf nf vapbeerpg nf vgf
Ratyvfu genafyngvba.
  Gurer ner guerr qvssrerag cyheny fhssvkrf va Xyvatba.

  {-ch'} <cyheny sbe orvatf pncnoyr bs hfvat ynathntr>

  Guvf fhssvk pna or hfrq gb vaqvpngr cyhenyvgl sbe Xyvatbaf,
Greenaf, Ebzhynaf, Ihypnaf, naq fb ba, ohg abg sbe ybjre
navznyf bs nal xvaq, cynagf, vanavzngr bowrpgf, ryrpgebznt-
argvp be bgure ornzf be jnirf, rgp. [[c.23]]

    {lnF} <bssvpre>   {lnFch'} <bssvpref>
    {Qhl} <rzvffnel>  {Qhlch'} <rzvffnevrf>

  {-Qh'} <cyheny sbe obql cnegf>

  Guvf fhssvk vf hfrq jura ersreevat gb obql cnegf bs gubfr
orvatf pncnoyr bs hfvat ynathntr nf jryy nf bs nal bgure
navzny.

    {dnz} <sbbg>       {dnzQh'} <srrg>
    {gyuba} <abfgevy>  {gyubaQh'} <abfgevyf>

  {-zrl} <cyheny, trareny hfntr>

  Guvf fhssvk vf hfrq gb znex gur cyheny bs nal abha.

    {zVQ} <pbybal>  {zVQzrl} <pbybavrf>
    {lhD} <cynarg>  {lhDzrl} <cynargf>

  Vg pna nyfb or hfrq jvgu abhaf ersreevat gb orvatf pncnoyr bs
hfvat ynathntr (gubfr abhaf juvpu gnxr {-ch'}). Jura vg vf fb
hfrq, vg nqqf n abgvba bs "fpnggrerq nyy nobhg" gb gur zrnavat.
Pbzcner:

    {chd} <puvyq>
    {chdch'} <puvyqera>
    {chdzrl} <puvyqera nyy bire gur cynpr>

  Gur fhssvk {-zrl} pnaabg or hfrq jvgu obql cnegf. Vg fubhyq
or abgrq, ubjrire, gung Xyvatba cbrgf bsgra ivbyngr guvf
tenzzngvpny ehyr va beqre gb ribxr cnegvphyne zbbqf va gurve
cbrgel. Guhf, sbezf fhpu nf {gyubazrl} <abfgevyf fpnggrerq nyy
nobhg> qb bpphe. Hagvy gur fhogyr ahnaprf bs fhpu pbafgehpgvbaf
ner svezyl tenfcrq, ubjrire, vg vf fhttrfgrq gung fghqragf bs
Xyvatba fgvpx gb gur ehyrf.

  Svanyyl, fbzr abhaf va Xyvatba ner vaureragyl be nyjnlf
cyheny va zrnavat, naq gurersber arire gnxr cyheny fhssvkrf.

    {enl'} <gnetrgf> [[c.24]]
    {pun} <gbecrqbrf>
    {puhlQnU} <guehfgref>

  Gur fvathyne pbhagrecnegf bs fhpu jbeqf ner hggreyl qvf-
gvapg:

    {QbF} <gnetrg>
    {crat} <gbecrqb>
    {iVw} <guehfgre>

  Gur fvathyne sbezf znl gnxr gur {-zrl} fhssvk, ohg gur
zrnavat nyjnlf pneevrf gur "fpnggrerq nyy nobhg" pbaabgngvba:

    {QbFzrl} <gnetrgf fpnggrerq nyy nobhg>
    {cratzrl} <gbecrqbrf nyy bire gur cynpr>

  Vaureragyl cyheny abhaf ner gerngrq tenzzngvpnyyl nf fvath-
yne abhaf va gung fvathyne cebabhaf ner hfrq gb ersre gb gurz
(frpgvbaf 4.1, 5.1). Sbe rknzcyr, va gur fragrapr {pun lVtuhF}
<Fgnaq ol gbecrqbrf!> be <Trg gur gbecrqbrf ernql gb or sverq!> gur
ireo cersvk {lV-,} na vzcrengvir cersvk hfrq sbe fvathyne bowrpgf,
zhfg or hfrq rira gubhtu gur bowrpg ({pun} <gbecrqbrf>) unf n
cyheny zrnavat.


3.3.3. Glcr 3: Dhnyvsvpngvba

Fhssvkrf bs guvf glcr vaqvpngr gur fcrnxre'f nggvghqr gbjneq gur
abha, be ubj fher gur fcrnxre vf gung gur abha vf orvat hfrq
nccebcevngryl.

  {-dbd} <fb-pnyyrq>

  Guvf fhssvk vaqvpngrf gung gur abha vf orvat hfrq va n snyfr be
vebavp snfuvba. Fnlvat {ebwdbd} <fb-pnyyrq crnpr,> engure guna
fvzcyl {ebw} <crnpr,> vaqvpngrf gung gur fcrnxre qbrf abg ernyyl
oryvrir gung crnpr vf yrtvgvzngr be yvxryl gb raqher.

  {-Url} <nccnerag>

  Guvf fhssvk vaqvpngrf gung gur fcrnxre vf cerggl fher gur
bowrpg ersreerq gb ol gur abha vf npphengryl qrfpevorq ol gur
abha, ohg unf fbzr qbhogf. Sbe rknzcyr, vs gur fpnaare ba n
Xyvatba fuvc frafrf na bowrpg, naq gur bssvpre ercbegvat gur
cerfrapr bs guvf bowrpg nffhzrf, ohg vf abg lrg fher, gung gur
bowrpg vf n irffry, ur jvyy cebonoyl ersre gb gur bowrpg nf
{QhwUrl} <na nccnerag irffry,> engure guna fvzcyl {Qhw} <irffry.> [[c.25]]

  {-an'} <qrsvavgr>

  Guvf vf gur pbhagrecneg bs {-Url.} Vg vaqvpngrf gung gurer vf ab
qbhog va gur fcrnxre'f zvaq nf gb gur npphenpl bs uvf be ure
pubvpr bs jbeqf. Bapr gur Xyvatba bssvpre ersreerq gb nobir vf
fher gung gur bowrpg gur fpnaare unf sbhaq vf n irffry, ur zvtug
ercbeg gur cerfrapr bs {Qhwan'} <n qrsvavgr irffry, haqbhogrqyl n
irffry.>


3.3.4. Glcr 4: Cbffrffvba/fcrpvsvpngvba

Glcr 4 vf gur ynetrfg pynff bs abha fhssvkrf. Vg pbafvfgf bs nyy gur
cbffrffvir fhssvkrf, cyhf fhssvkrf juvpu pna or genafyngrq nf
Ratyvfu <guvf> naq <gung.>

  Gur cbffrffvir fhssvkrf ner:

  {-jVw} <zl>             {-znw} <bhe>
  {-yVw} <lbhe>           {-enw} <lbhe (cyheny)>
  {-Qnw} <uvf, ure, vgf>  {-punw} <gurve>

  Guhf, {whU} <ubzr> bpphef va {whUjVw} <zl ubzr,> {whUyVw} <lbhe
ubzr,> {whUpunw} <gurve ubzr,> rgp.
  Jura gur abha orvat cbffrffrq ersref gb n orvat pncnoyr bs
hfvat ynathntr, n fcrpvny frg bs fhssvkrf vf hfrq sbe svefg- naq
frpbaq-crefba cbffrffbef:

  {-jV'} <zl>    {-zn'} <bhe>
  {-yV'} <lbhe>  {-en'} <lbhe (cyheny)>

  Gurfr fhssvkrf bpphe va, sbe rknzcyr, {wbUjV'} <zl ybeq> naq
{chdyV'} <lbhe puvyq.> Vg vf tenzzngvpnyyl pbeerpg gb hfr gur
erthyne cbffrffvir fhssvkrf jvgu abhaf ersreevat gb orvatf
pncnoyr bs fcrrpu (nf va {chdyVw} <lbhe puvyq>), ohg fhpu pba-
fgehpgvbaf ner pbafvqrerq qrebtngbel; {wbUjVw} sbe <zl ybeq>
obeqref ba gur gnobb. Fghqragf bs Xyvatba fubhyq orne guvf
va zvaq.
  Gb vaqvpngr gung bar abha vf gur cbffrffbe bs nabgure abha
(r.t., <rarzl'f jrncba>), ab fhssvk vf hfrq. Vafgrnq, gur gjb
abhaf ner fnvq va gur beqre cbffrffbe-cbffrffrq: {wntu ahU}
<rarzl'f jrncba> (yvgrenyyl, <rarzl jrncba>). Guvf pbafgehpgvba
vf nyfb hfrq sbe cuenfrf genafyngrq ol <bs gur> va Ratyvfu, fhpu nf
<jrncba bs gur rarzl.> (Frr nyfb frpgvba 3.4.) [[c.26]]

  Gurer ner gjb fhssvkrf vaqvpngvat ubj pybfr gb gur fcrnxre
gur bowrpg ersreerq gb ol gur abha vf.

  {-inz} <guvf>

  Yvxr vgf Ratyvfu genafyngvba, guvf fhssvk vaqvpngrf gung gur
abha ersref gb na bowrpg juvpu vf arneol be juvpu vf gur gbcvp
bs gur pbairefngvba.

    {ahUinz} <guvf jrncba (arne zr nf V fcrnx)>
    {lhDinz} <guvf cynarg (gung jr'ir orra gnyxvat nobhg)>

Jura hfrq jvgu n cyheny abha (bar jvgu n cyheny fhssvk be na
vaureragyl cyheny abha), {-inz} vf genafyngrq <gurfr:>

    {ahUzrlinz} <gurfr jrncbaf> [[\a:=\a\a]]
  {-irgyu} <gung>

  Guvf fhssvk vaqvpngrf gung gur abha ersref gb na bowrpg juvpu
vf abg arneol be juvpu vf orvat oebhtug hc ntnva nf gur gbcvp
bs pbairefngvba.

    {ahUirgyu} <gung jrncba (bire gurer)>
    {lhDirgyu} <gung cynarg (nf bccbfrq gb gur bar jr jrer whfg
               gnyxvat nobhg)>

Jura hfrq jvgu n cyheny abha, {-irgyu} vf genafyngrq <gubfr:>

    {ahUzrlirgyu} <gubfr jrncbaf>

  Gurer vf ab Xyvatba rdhvinyrag sbe Ratyvfu <n, na, gur.> Va
genafyngvat sebz Xyvatba gb Ratyvfu, bar zhfg hfr pbagrkg nf
n thvqr gb jura gb hfr <n> be <na> naq jura <gur.> Va guvf obbx, <n> be
<na> naq <gur> ner hfrq va genafyngvbaf gb znxr gur Ratyvfu fbhaq
zber angheny.


3.3.5. Glcr 5: Flagnpgvp znexref

Gurfr fhssvkrf vaqvpngr fbzrguvat nobhg gur shapgvba bs gur
abha va gur fragrapr. Nf va Ratyvfu, fhowrpgf naq bowrpgf ner
abeznyyl vaqvpngrq ol gur cbfvgvba bs gur abha be abhaf va
gur fragrapr. Gur sbyybjvat gjb Ratyvfu fragraprf unir gur
fnzr jbeqf, ohg gur fragraprf unir qvssrerag zrnavatf qhr gb
gur beqre bs gur jbeqf:

  <Qbtf punfr pngf.>
  <Pngf punfr qbtf.> [[c.27]]

Fhowrpgf naq bowrpgf va Xyvatba ner yvxrjvfr vaqvpngrq ol
jbeq beqre. Guvf vf qrfpevorq va frpgvba 6.1.
  Va bgure vafgnaprf, Ratyvfu vaqvpngrf gur shapgvba bs abhaf
va n fragrapr ol nqqvat jbeqf, cnegvphyneyl cercbfvgvbaf. Va
gur sbyybjvat Ratyvfu fragrapr, gur jbeq <nebhaq> orsber
<pnanevrf> vaqvpngrf gung gur pnanevrf ner arvgure punfvat abe
orvat punfrq:

  <Qbtf punfr pngf nebhaq pnanevrf.>

  Fvzvyneyl, va Xyvatba, abhaf juvpu vaqvpngr fbzrguvat
bgure guna fhowrpg be bowrpg hfhnyyl zhfg unir fbzr fcrpvny
vaqvpngvba bs rknpgyl jung gurve shapgvba vf. Hayvxr Ratyvfu,
guvf vf nppbzcyvfurq ol hfvat fhssvkrf.

  {-Qnd} <ybpngvir>

  Guvf fhssvk vaqvpngrf gung fbzrguvat vf unccravat (be unf
unccrarq be jvyy unccra) va gur ivpvavgl bs gur abha gb juvpu
vg vf nggnpurq. Vg vf abeznyyl genafyngrq ol na Ratyvfu cercbfv-
gvba: <gb, va, ng, ba.> Gur rknpg genafyngvba vf qrgrezvarq ol gur
zrnavat bs gur jubyr fragrapr. Sbe rknzcyr, {cn'Qnd} vf {cn'}
<ebbz> cyhf gur fhssvk {-Qnd.} Vg znl bpphe va fragraprf fhpu nf
gur sbyybjvat:

    {cn'Qnd wVUgnU} <V'z va gur ebbz.>
    {cn'Qnd lVwnU} <Tb gb gur ebbz!>

Va gur svefg fragrapr, {wVU} <V> vf hfrq va gur frafr bs <V nz> (frr
frpgvba 6.3), fb <va> vf gur zbfg ernfbanoyr genafyngvba bs {-Qnd.}
Va gur frpbaq fragrapr, gur ireo vf {wnU} <tb,> fb <gb> znxrf gur
zbfg frafr nf n genafyngvba bs {-Qnd.} Na Ratyvfu cercbfvgvba
arrq abg or cneg bs gur genafyngvba. Xyvatba {Qhat} zrnaf <nern
nobir,> naq {QhatQnd} vf <bireurnq,> yvgrenyyl fbzrguvat yvxr "ng
gur nern nobir." Sbe shegure qvfphffvba ba cercbfvgvbany
pbaprcgf, frr frpgvba 3.4.
  Vg vf jbegu abgvat ng guvf cbvag gung gur pbaprcgf rkcerffrq
ol gur Ratyvfu nqireof <urer, gurer,> naq <rireljurer> ner
rkcerffrq ol abhaf va Xyvatba: {anQri} <urernobhgf,> {cn'} <gurer-
nobhgf,> {Qng} <rireljurer.> Gurfr jbeqf znl creuncf or genaf-
yngrq zber yvgrenyyl nf "nern nebhaq urer," "nern bire gurer,"
naq "nyy cynprf," erfcrpgviryl. Hayvxr bgure abhaf, gurfr
guerr jbeqf ner arire sbyybjrq ol gur ybpngvir fhssvk. (Abgr [[c.28]]
gung {cn'} <gurernobhgf> naq {cn'} <ebbz> ner vqragvpny va fbhaq;
{cn'Qnd,} ubjrire, pna zrna bayl <va/gb gur ebbz.>)
  Gurer ner n srj ireof jubfr zrnavatf vapyhqr ybpngvir
abgvbaf, fhpu nf {tubF} <nccebnpu, cebprrq.> Gur ybpngvir fhssvk
arrq abg or hfrq ba abhaf juvpu ner gur bowrpgf bs fhpu
ireof.

    {Qhw tubFgnU} <Vg vf nccebnpuvat gur fuvc.>
                  ({Qhw} <fuvc, irffry,> {tubFgnU} <vg vf
                  nccebnpuvat vg>)

    {lhD jVtubFgnU} <Jr ner cebprrqvat gbjneq gur cynarg.>
                    ({lhD} <cynarg,> {iVtubFgnU} <jr ner
                    cebprrqvat gbjneq vg>)

Vs gur ybpngvir fhssvk vf hfrq jvgu fhpu ireof, gur erfhygvat
fragrapr vf fbzrjung erqhaqnag, ohg abg bhg-naq-bhg jebat.

    {QhwQnd tubFgnU} <Vg vf nccebnpuvat gbjneq gur fuvc.>

  {-ib'} <sebz>

  Guvf fhssvk vf fvzvyne gb {-Qnd} ohg vf hfrq bayl jura npgvba vf
va n qverpgvba njnl sebz gur abha fhssvkrq jvgu {-ib'.}

    {cn'ib' lVwnU} <Yrnir gur ebbz!>

N zber yvgreny genafyngvba bs guvf fragrapr zvtug or "Tb sebz
gur ebbz." [[.:=!]]

  {-zb'} <qhr gb, orpnhfr bs>

  Guvf fhssvk bpphef va fragraprf fhpu nf:

    {FhFzb' wbdgnU} <Vg vf syhggrevat va gur oerrmr.>

  Gur abha {FhFzb'} zrnaf <qhr gb gur oerrmr,> fb gur jubyr
fragrapr vf yvgrenyyl "qhr gb gur oerrmr, vg [n synt] vf syhggre-
vat."

  {-inQ} <sbe, vagraqrq sbe>

  Guvf fhssvk vaqvpngrf gung gur abha gb juvpu vg vf nggnpurq vf
va fbzr jnl gur orarsvpvnel bs gur npgvba, gur crefba be guvat
sbe jubz be sbe juvpu gur npgvivgl bpphef.

    {Dh'inQ yV' Qr'inz} <Guvf vasbezngvba vf hfrshy sbe
                        gur zvffvba.> [[c.29]]

Gur abha {Dh'inQ} zrnaf <sbe gur zvffvba,> naq va guvf fragrapr
{-inQ} vaqvpngrf gung gur vasbezngvba vf vagraqrq gb or hfrq
fbzrubj sbe gur zvffvba haqre qvfphffvba.

  {-'r'} <gbcvp>

  Guvf fhssvk rzcunfvmrf gung gur abha gb juvpu vg vf nggnpurq
vf gur gbcvp bs gur fragrapr. Va Ratyvfu, guvf vf serdhragyl
nppbzcyvfurq ol fgerffvat gur abha (fnlvat vg rzcungvpnyyl) be
ol fcrpvny flagnpgvp pbafgehpgvbaf.

    {yhwch' wVU'r'} <V, naq bayl V, unir snvyrq.> [[yhwch':=wVyhwch']]
                    <Vg vf V jub unf snvyrq.>

    {Qr''r' iVgyuncaVFch'} <V arrqrq gb trg gur VASBEZNGVBA.>
                           <Vg jnf gur vasbezngvba (naq abg
                           fbzrguvat ryfr) gung V arrqrq.>

Jvgubhg gur {'r',} gurfr fnzr fragraprf jbhyq unir ab abha [['r':=-'r']]
fvatyrq bhg sbe rzcunfvf:

    {yhwch' wVU} <V unir snvyrq.> [[yhwch':=wVyhwch']]
    {Qr' iVgyuncaVFch'} <V arrqrq gb trg gur vasbezngvba.>

  Sbe n shegure hfr bs {-'r',} frr frpgvba 6.3.


3.3.6. Eryngvir beqrevat bs gur fhssvkrf

Nf oevrsyl vyyhfgengrq va gur qvfphffvba bs {-inz} <guvf> naq {-irgyu}
<gung> (frpgvba 3.3.4), jura n abha vf sbyybjrq ol zber guna
bar fhssvk, gur fhssvkrf zhfg bpphe va gur cebcre beqre,
nppbeqvat gb gur pynffvsvpngvba whfg qrfpevorq. Vg vf ener sbe n
abha gb or sbyybjrq ol svir fhssvkrf, ohg vg qbrf unccra sebz
gvzr gb gvzr. Fbzr rknzcyrf bs abhaf jvgu gjb be zber
fhssvkrf sbyybj. (Fhssvk glcrf ner vaqvpngrq ol ahzoref.)

    {DntuUbzzrlUrlyVwzb'} <qhr gb lbhe nccnerag zvabe reebef>
      {Dntu}  (abha)  <reebe>
      {-Ubz}  (1)     <qvzvahgvir>
      {-zrl}  (2)     <cyheny>
      {-Url}  (3)     <nccnerag>
      {-yVw}  (4)     <lbhe>
      {-zb'}  (5)     <qhr gb>

    {cn'jVwQnd} <va zl dhnegref>
      {cn'}   (abha)  <ebbz> [[c.30]]
      {-jVw}  (4)     <zl>
      {-Qnd}  (5)     <ybpngvir>

    {Qhlch'dbdpunw} <gurve fb-pnyyrq rzvffnevrf>
      {Qhl}    (abha)  <rzvffnel>
      {-ch'}   (2)     <cyheny>
      {-dbd}   (3)     <fb-pnyyrq>
      {-punw}  (4)     <gurve>

    {dnzQh'jVwQnd} <ng zl srrg>
      {dnz}   (abha)  <sbbg>
      {-Qh'}  (2)     <cyheny>
      {-jVw}  (4)     <zl>
      {-Qnd}  (5)     <ybpngvir>

    {ebwUbz'r'} <gur gehpr> (nf gbcvp)
      {ebw}   (abha)  <crnpr>
      {-Ubz}  (1)     <qvzvahgvir>
      {-'r'}  (5)     <gbcvp>

  Nyy rknzcyrf bs fhssvkrf tvira fb sne fubj bayl fvzcyr
abhaf. Fhssvkrf ner nggnpurq gb pbzcyrk abhaf (frpgvba 3.2) va
rknpgyl gur fnzr snfuvba.

    {QViV'znl'QhwzrlQnd} <ng/gb gur Srqrengvba onggyr pehvfref>
      {QViV'znl'Qhw}  (abha)  <Srqrengvba onggyr pehvfre>
      {-zrl}          (2)     <cyheny>
      {-Qnd}          (5)     <ybpngvir>

    {onUjV'ch'inz} <gurfr thaaref>
      {onUjV'}  (abha)  <thaare>
      {-ch'}    (2)     <cyheny>
      {-inz}    (4)     <guvf>


3.4. Gur abha--abha pbafgehpgvba

Fbzr pbzovangvbaf bs gjb (be zber) abhaf va n ebj ner fb
pbzzba nf gb unir orpbzr rirelqnl jbeqf. Gurfr ner gur
pbzcbhaq abhaf (nf qvfphffrq va frpgvba 3.2.1). Va nqqvgvba,
vg vf cbffvoyr gb pbzovar abhaf va gur znaare bs n pbzcbhaq
abha gb cebqhpr n arj pbafgehpg rira vs vg vf abg n yrtvgvzngr
pbzcbhaq abha ("yrtvgvzngr" va gur frafr gung vg jbhyq or
sbhaq va n qvpgvbanel).
  Gur genafyngvba bs gjb abhaf pbzovarq va guvf jnl, fnl [[c.31]]
A1-A2 (gung vf, abha #1 sbyybjrq ol abha #2), jbhyq or <A2
bs gur A1.> Sbe rknzcyr, {ahU} <jrncba> naq {crtu} <frperg> pbzovar
gb sbez {ahU crtu} <frperg bs gur jrncba.> Na nygreangr genafyn-
gvba jbhyq or <A1'f A2,> va guvf pnfr, <gur jrncba'f frperg.> Nf
qvfphffrq va frpgvba 3.3.4, guvf vf gur Xyvatba cbffrffvir
pbafgehpgvba sbe n abha cbffrffrq ol nabgure abha.
  Jura gur abha-abha pbafgehpgvba vf hfrq, bayl gur frpbaq
abha pna gnxr flagnpgvp fhssvkrf (Glcr 5). Obgu abhaf,
ubjrire, znl gnxr fhssvkrf bs gur bgure sbhe glcrf. Sbe
rknzcyr:

    {ahUinz crtu} <frperg bs guvf jrncba>
      {ahU}   (abha)  <jrncba>
      {-inz}  (4)     <guvf>
      {crtu}  (abha)  <frperg>

    {wntuch' lhDzrlQnd} <ng/gb gur rarzvrf' cynargf>
      {wntu}  (abha)  <rarzl>
      {-ch'}  (2)     <cyheny>
      {lhD}   (abha)  <cynarg>
      {-zrl}  (2)     <cyheny>
      {-Qnd}  (5)     <ybpngvir>

    {chdjV' dnzQh'} <zl puvyq'f srrg>
      {chd}   (abha)  <puvyq>
      {-jV'}  (4)     <zl>
      {dnz}   (abha)  <sbbg>
      {-Qh}   (2)     <cyheny>

  Ratyvfu cercbfvgvbany cuenfrf ner nyfb eraqrerq va Xyvatba
ol guvf abha-abha pbafgehpgvba. Cercbfvgvbany pbaprcgf fhpu
nf nobir naq orybj ner npghnyyl abhaf va Xyvatba, orfg
genafyngrq nf "nern nobir," "nern orybj," rgp. Gur ybpngvir
fhssvk (frpgvba 3.3.5) sbyybjf gur frpbaq abha. Sbe rknzcyr:

    {antu QhatQnd} <nobir gur ebpx>
      {antu}  (abha)  <ebpx>
      {Qhat}  (abha)  <nern nobir>
      {-Qnd}  (5)     <ybpngvir>

Zber yvgrenyyl, guvf vf "ng gur nern nobir gur ebpx" be "ng gur
ebpx'f nobir-nern." [[c.32]]


4. IREOF

Xyvatba ireof ner zbfgyl zbabflyynovp sbezf juvpu znl
or nppbzcnavrq ol frireny nssvkrf. Nf jvgu Xyvatba
abhaf, Xyvatba ireof znl gnxr fhssvkrf snyyvat vagb n ahzore
bs glcrf onfrq ba gurve eryngvir cbfvgvba sbyybjvat gur ireo.
Gurer ner avar glcrf bs ireo fhssvkrf. Hayvxr Xyvatba
abhaf, Xyvatba ireof znl gnxr cersvkrf. Guhf, vs fhssvk glcrf
ner vaqvpngrq nf ahzoref, gur fgehpgher bs n Xyvatba ireo
vf:

  CERSVK--IREO--1--2--3--4--5--6--7--8--9


4.1. Cebabzvany cersvkrf

Rnpu Xyvatba ireo ortvaf jvgu n fvatyr cersvk gung vaqvpngrf
jub be jung vf cresbezvat gur npgvba qrfpevorq ol gur ireo
naq, jura eryrinag, jub be jung vf gur erpvcvrag bs gung
npgvba. Va bgure jbeqf, Xyvatba ireo cersvkrf vaqvpngr obgu
gur fhowrpg naq gur bowrpg bs gur fragrapr.


4.1.1. Onfvp cersvkrf

Gur onfvp frg bs cersvkrf pna or cerfragrq va n puneg. (Va beqre
gb znxr gur puneg nf pyrne nf cbffvoyr, fbzr cersvkrf ner
ercrngrq.)
  Abgr gung obgu gur fhowrpg naq gur bowrpg ner pbzovarq [[c.33]]

  BOWRPG         abar   <zr>   <lbh>  <uvz/> <hf>   <lbh>  <gurz>
                                     <ure/vg>     <(cyheny)>
  FHOWRPG
  <V>            {wV-}  --     {dn-}  {iV-}  --     {Fn-}  {iV-}

  <lbh>          {oV-}  {pub-} --     {Qn-}  {wh-}  --     {Qn-}

  <ur/fur/vg>    0      {zh-}  {Qh-}  0      {ah-}  {yV-}  0

  <jr>           {zn-}  --     {cV-}  {jV-}  --     {er-}  {QV-}

  <lbh (cyheny)> {Fh-}  {gh-}  --     {ob-}  {pur-} --     {ob-}

  <gurl>         0      {zh-}  {aV-}  {yh-}  {ah-}  {yV-}  0

vagb n fvatyr cersvk. 0 va gur puneg zrnaf gung gur cnegvphyne
fhowrpg-bowrpg pbzovangvbaf ner vaqvpngrq ol gur nofrapr bs n
cersvk orsber gur ireo; -- va gur puneg abgrf fhowrpg-bowrpg
pbzovangvbaf juvpu pnaabg or rkcerffrq jvgu gur Xyvatba
ireo cersvk flfgrz. Sbe fhpu zrnavatf, fhssvkrf (frpgvba 4.2.1)
naq/be cebabhaf (frpgvba 5.1) zhfg or hfrq.
  Gur cersvkrf va gur svefg pbyhza bs gur puneg (urnqrq
"abar") ner hfrq jura gurer vf ab bowrpg; gung vf, jura gur
npgvba bs gur ireo nssrpgf bayl gur fhowrpg (gur "qbre"). Gur
ireo {Dbat} <fyrrc> bpphef jvgu gur cebabzvany cersvkrf nf
sbyybjf:

    {wVDbat} <V fyrrc>
    {oVDbat} <lbh fyrrc>
    {Dbat} <ur/fur/vg fyrrcf, gurl fyrrc>
    {znDbat} <jr fyrrc>
    {FhDbat} <lbh (cyheny) fyrrc>

Va gur pnfr bs {Dbat} <ur/fur/vg fyrrcf, gurl fyrrc,> gur rknpg
fhowrpg jbhyq or vaqvpngrq ryfrjurer va gur fragrapr be ol
pbagrkg.
  Guvf frg bs cersvkrf vf nyfb hfrq jura na bowrpg vf cbffvoyr,
ohg haxabja be inthr. Guhf, {wVlnw} <V haqrefgnaq> pna or hfrq [[c.34]]
jura gur fcrnxre haqrefgnaqf guvatf va trareny, xabjf jung
vf tbvat ba, be haqrefgnaqf jung nabgure fcrnxre unf whfg
fnvq. Vg pnaabg, ubjrire, or hfrq sbe haqrefgnaqvat n yna-
thntr be haqrefgnaqvat n crefba. Fvzvyneyl, {znFbc} <jr rng> pna
or hfrq gb vaqvpngr n trareny npg bs rngvat, ohg abg vs n fcrpvsvp
sbbq vf zragvbarq.
  Gur erznvavat cersvkrf pbzovar fhowrpg naq bowrpg. Fbzr
bs gurz ner vyyhfgengrq orybj, hfvat gur ireo {yrtu} <frr.>

    {dnyrtu} <V frr lbh>           {pubyrtu} <lbh frr zr>
    {iVyrtu} <V frr uvz/ure/vg/    {zhyrtu} <ur/fur/vg frrf zr,>
             gurz>                          <gurl frr zr>
    {Fnyrtu} <V frr lbh (cyheny)>  {ghyrtu} <lbh (cyheny) frr zr>

    {Qnyrtu} <lbh frr uvz/ure/     {Qhyrtu} <ur/fur/vg frrf lbh>
             vg/gurz>
    {whyrtu} <lbh frr hf>          {cVyrtu} <jr frr lbh>

    {yrtu} <ur/fur/vg frrf         {yhyrtu} <gurl frr uvz/ure/vg>
           uvz/ure/vg/gurz,>
           <gurl frr gurz>


4.1.2 Vzcrengvir cersvkrf [[4.1.2:=4.1.2.]]

N fcrpvny frg bs cersvkrf vf hfrq sbe vzcrengvirf, gung vf, ireof
tvivat pbzznaqf. Pbzznaqf pna or tvira bayl gb <lbh> be <lbh
(cyheny).>

  BOWRPG          abar   <zr>   <uvz/ure/vg>  <hf>    <gurz>

  <lbh>           {lV-}  {UV-}  {lV-}         {tub-}  {gV-}
  <lbh (cyheny)>  {cr-}  {UV-}  {lV-}         {tub-}  {gV-}

  Abgr gung, jvgu bar rkprcgvba, gur vqragvpny cersvk vf hfrq
ertneqyrff bs jurgure gur pbzznaq vf orvat tvira gb bar be
zber guna bar crefba. Gur fvatyr rkprcgvba vf jura n
pbzznaq vf tvira ohg gurer vf ab bowrpg. Va fhpu pnfrf, n
fcrpvny cersvk {cr-} vf hfrq gb tvir n pbzznaq gb frireny crbcyr.
Rknzcyrf bs gur vzcrengvir cersvkrf sbyybj. Rkpynzngvba
cbvagf va gur genafyngvba vaqvpngr gung vg vf n pbzznaq.

    {lVDbat} <fyrrc!>          {crDbat} <(lbh cyheny) fyrrc!>

    {UVdVc} <uvg zr!>          {tubdVc} <uvg hf!> [[c.35]]

    {lVdVc} <uvg uvz/ure/vg!>  {gVdVc} <uvg gurz!>

  Gb vaqvpngr npgvba qverpgrq ntnvafg barfrys va na vzcrengvir
ireo (r.t., <gryy lbhefrys>), gur fhssvk {-rtu} <barfrys> vf hfrq nybat [[-rtu:=-'rtu]]
jvgu {lV-} be {cr-} (frr frpgvba 4.2.1).


4.1.3 Abgngvbany pbairagvbaf [[4.1.3:=4.1.3.]]

Nf n abgngvbany pbairagvba, cersvkrf vaqvpngvat fhowrpg naq
bowrpg jvyy or genafyngrq nf <fhowrpg--bowrpg;> r.t., {dn-} <V--lbh,>
{cV-} <jr--gurz.> Vzcrengvir cersvkrf jvyy or genafyngrq fvzvyneyl,
cerprqrq ol gur jbeq <vzcrengvir:> {gV-} <vzcrengvir: lbh--gurz.>
  Nyfb, cersvkrf juvpu pna ersre gb znyr, srznyr, vanavzngr,
fvathyne, naq/be cyheny (r.t., {iV-} <V--uvz/ure/vg/gurz>) jvyy or
genafyngrq pbeerpgyl, ohg hfhnyyl jvgubhg tvivat nyy gur bcgvbaf
(r.t., <V--uvz/ure>). Guvf pbairagvba jvyy nyfb or hfrq jura
genafyngvat ireof pbagnvavat gurfr cersvkrf; r.t., {iVyrtu} <V frr
uvz/ure.>


4.2. Ireo fhssvkrf

Gurer ner avar glcrf bs ireo fhssvkrf.


4.2.1. Glcr 1: Barfrys/bar nabgure

  {-rtu} <barfrys> [[-rtu:=-'rtu]]

  Guvf fhssvk vf hfrq gb vaqvpngr gung gur npgvba qrfpevorq ol
gur ireo nssrpgf gur cresbezre bs gur npgvba, gur fhowrpg. Vg vf
genafyngrq ol Ratyvfu <frys.> Jura guvf fhssvk vf hfrq, gur cersvk
frg vaqvpngvat "ab bowrpg" zhfg nyfb or hfrq.

    {wVdVc'rtu} <V uvg zlfrys> ({dVc} <uvg>)
    {oVdVc'rtu} <lbh uvg lbhefrys>
    {dVc'rtu} <ur/fur uvgf uvzfrys/urefrys>

  Vg vf nyfb cbffvoyr gb hfr guvf fhssvk jvgu vzcrengvir ireof.
Nf jvgu abavzcrengvirf, gur cersvk vaqvpngvat "ab bowrpg"
zhfg or hfrq.

    {lVwn''rtu} <gryy lbhefrys!> ({wn'} <gryy>)
    {crwn''rtu} <gryy lbhefryirf!> [[c.36]]

  {-puhd} <bar nabgure>

  Guvf fhssvk vf hfrq bayl jvgu cyheny fhowrpgf. Vg vf genafyngrq
<rnpu bgure> be <bar nabgure.> Gur cersvk frg vaqvpngvat "ab
bowrpg" vf nyfb hfrq jura guvf fhssvk vf hfrq.

    {zndVcpuhd} <jr uvg rnpu bgure> ({dVc} <uvg>)
    {FhdVcpuhd} <lbh (cyheny) uvg rnpu bgure>
    {dVcpuhd} <gurl uvg rnpu bgure>
    {crdVcpuhd} <uvg rnpu bgure!>


4.2.2. Glcr 2: Ibyvgvba/cerqvfcbfvgvba

Fhssvkrf bs guvf glcr rkcerff ubj zhpu pubvpr gur fhowrpg unf
nobhg gur npgvba qrfpevorq be ubj cerqvfcbfrq gur fhowrpg vf
gb qbvat vg.

  {-aVF} <arrq>

    {iVyrtuaVF} <V arrq gb frr uvz/ure> ({yrtu} <frr>)
    {oVFbcaVF} <lbh arrq gb rng> ({Fbc} <rng>)

  {-dnat} <jvyyvat>

    {Urtudnat} <ur/fur vf jvyyvat gb qvr> ({Urtu} <qvr>)
    {dnwn'dnat} <V nz jvyyvat gb gryy lbh> ({wn'} <gryy>)

  {-ehc} <ernql, cercnerq> (ersreevat gb orvatf)

    {Urtuehc} <ur/fur vf ernql gb qvr> ({Urtu} <qvr>)
    {dnyrtuehc} <V nz ernql gb frr lbh> ({yrtu} <frr>)
    {ahwn'ehc} <gurl ner cercnerq gb gryy hf> ({wn'} <gryy>)

  {-orU} <ernql, frg hc> (ersreevat gb qrivprf)

    {cbworU} <(gur qrivpr) vf frg hc gb nanylmr vg> ({cbw} <nanylmr>)
    {ynoorU} <(gur qrivpr) vf ernql gb genafzvg qngn> ({yno}
             <genafzvg qngn>)

  Gurer vf, vg fubhyq or abgrq, n ireo {tuhF} juvpu zrnaf <gb or
cercnerq gb ynhapu be cebwrpg (fbzrguvat).> Guvf ireo arire
gnxrf gur fhssvk {-ehc.} Vg vf hfrq cevznevyl va ersrerapr gb
gbecrqbrf---fb zhpu fb gung vs gur bowrpg vf abg fcrpvsvpnyyl [[c.37]]
fgngrq, naq pbagrkg qbrf abg qvpgngr bgurejvfr, vg vf nyjnlf
nffhzrq gb or <gbecrqbrf.> Nppbeqvatyl, obgu bs gur sbyybjvat
fragraprf zrna <Or cercnerq gb ynhapu gbecrqbrf!> be <Fgnaq ol
ba gbecrqbrf!>

    {pun lVtuhF}  ({pun} <gbecrqbrf>)
    {lVtuhF}

  Gur ireo {tuhF} pna nyfb or hfrq va ersrerapr gb, nzbat
bgure guvatf, ebpxrgf, zvffvyrf, naq inevbhf xvaqf bs raretl
ornzf (juvpu, yvxr gbecrqbrf, tb sebz bar cbvag gb nabgure).
Vg vf nyfb hfrq gb qrfpevor gur npgvba bs chyyvat onpx gur rynfgvp
onaq bs n fyvatfubg. Va zbfg bgure vafgnaprf bs cercnerqarff,
ubjrire, {-ehc} vf erdhverq.

  {-iVc} <nsenvq>

    {pubUbUiVc} <lbh ner nsenvq gb xvyy zr> ({UbU} <xvyy>)
    {zhdVciVc} <gurl ner nsenvq gb uvg hf> ({dVc} <uvg>)

  Guvf fhssvk vf eneryl hfrq jvgu n cersvk zrnavat <V> be <jr.>
Gubhtu vg vf tenzzngvpnyyl pbeerpg, vg vf phyghenyyl gnobb.


4.2.3. Glcr 3: Punatr

Fhssvkrf bs guvf glcr vaqvpngr gung gur npgvba qrfpevorq ol gur
ireo vaibyirf n punatr bs fbzr xvaq sebz gur fgngr bs nssnvef
gung rkvfgrq orsber gur npgvba gbbx cynpr.

  {-pubU} <punatr va fgngr, punatr va qverpgvba>

    {znQb'pubU} <jr ner orpbzvat yhpxl, jr ner haqretbvat
                n ghea bs yhpx> ({Qb'} <or yhpxl>)
    {tubFpubU} <ur/fur vf ortvaavat gb tb (fbzrjurer)>
               ({tubF} <tb>)

  Gur vzcyvpngvba bs gur frpbaq rknzcyr vf gung ur be fur jnf
tbvat rvgure abjurer be fbzrjurer ryfr fbzrgvzr orsber gur
cuenfr jnf hggrerq. Abgr gung gur genafyngvba bs guvf fhssvk
znl or Ratyvfu <orpbzr> be <ortva gb.>

  {-dn'} <erfhzr>

  Hfvat guvf fhssvk vzcyvrf gung na npgvba unq orra gnxvat
cynpr, gura vg fgbccrq, naq gura vg ortna ntnva.

    {iVarwdn'} <V nz erfhzvat gur frnepu, V nz frnepuvat sbe [[c.38]]
               uvz/ure ntnva> ({arw} <frnepu>)


4.2.4. Glcr 4: Pnhfr

  {-zbU} <pnhfr>

  Nqqvat guvf fhssvk gb n ireo vaqvpngrf gung gur fhowrpg vf
pnhfvat n punatr bs pbaqvgvba be pnhfvat n arj pbaqvgvba gb
pbzr vagb rkvfgrapr.

    {gVwjV'tubz iVpurazbU} <V sbez n obneqvat cnegl>
                           ({gVwjV'tubz} <obneqvat cnegl,>
                           {pura} <gnxr sbez, gnxr funcr>)

Guvf fragrapr zvtug nyfb or genafyngrq <V pnhfr n obneqvat
cnegl gb or sbezrq.>

    {UVDblzbU} <yrg zr urne (fbzrguvat)> ({Dbl} <urne>) [[(fbzrguvat):=(fbzrguvat)!]]

Zber erirnyvatyl, guvf fragrapr pbhyq or genafyngrq <pnhfr zr
gb urne (fbzrguvat).> Abgr gung guvf fragrapr jbhyq abg or
hfrq va nfxvat crezvffvba gb urne; vg vf n qverpg pbzznaq.
  Abeznyyl, gur orfg Ratyvfu genafyngvba bs n ireo jvgu {-zbU}
qbrf abg pbagnva gur jbeq <pnhfr.> Sbe rknzcyr, {purazbU}
<ur/fur znxrf, perngrf> pbhyq or genafyngrq <ur/fur pnhfrf gb gnxr
funcr> ({pura} <gnxr sbez, gnxr funcr>), ohg guvf vf na njxjneq
Ratyvfu cuenfr.


4.2.5. Glcr 5: Vaqrsvavgr fhowrpg/novyvgl

Gur gjb fhssvkrf bs Glcr 5 unir abguvat zhpu gb qb jvgu rnpu
bgure rkprcg sbe obgu orvat Glcr 5. Nf n erfhyg, ab ireo
bpphef jvgu obgu bs gurfr fhssvkrf ng gur fnzr gvzr.

  {-yh'} <vaqrsvavgr fhowrpg>

  Guvf fhssvk vf hfrq gb vaqvpngr gung gur fhowrpg vf haxabja,
vaqrsvavgr, naq/be trareny. Fvapr gur fhowrpg vf nyjnlf gur
fnzr (gung vf, vg vf nyjnlf hafgngrq), gur cebabzvany cersvkrf
(frpgvba 4.1.1) ner hfrq va n qvssrerag jnl. Gubfr cersvkrf
juvpu abeznyyl vaqvpngr svefg- be frpbaq-crefba fhowrpg naq [[c.39]]
guveq-crefba fvathyne bowrpg ({iV-, Qn-, jV-, ob-}) ner hfrq gb
vaqvpngr svefg- be frpbaq-crefba bowrpg. Guhf, {iV-,} juvpu
abeznyyl zrnaf <V qb fbzrguvat gb uvz/ure,> jura va n ireo
jvgu {-yh'} zrnaf <fbzrbar/fbzrguvat qbrf fbzrguvat gb zr.>
Fvzvyneyl, gur cersvk {yh-,} juvpu abeznyyl zrnaf <gurl qb
fbzrguvat gb uvz/ure,> orpbzrf <fbzrbar/fbzrguvat qbrf
fbzrguvat gb gurz.>

    {Qndnjyh'} <fbzrbar/fbzrguvat erzrzoref lbh>
               ({dnj} <erzrzore>)
    {jVyrtuyh'} <fbzrbar/fbzrguvat frrf hf> ({yrtu} <frr>)
    {Fbcyh'} <fbzrbar/fbzrguvat rngf vg> ({Fbc} <rng>)

  Ireof jvgu {-yh'} ner bsgra genafyngrq vagb gur Ratyvfu cnffvir
ibvpr.

    {Qndnjyh'} <lbh ner erzrzorerq>
    {jVyrtuyh'} <jr ner frra>
    {Fbcyh'} <vg vf rngra>

  Jura hfrq jvgu gur ireo {gh'} <svaq, bofreir> naq n guveq- [[xrrc ulcura]]
crefba fvathyne fhowrpg cebabha (0), gur erfhygvat ireo sbez [[cebabha:=cersvk]]
{gh'yh'} <fbzrbar/fbzrguvat svaqf vg> vf bsgra genafyngrq ol Ra-
tyvfu <gurer vf.>

    {anQri chdch' gh'yh'} <gurer ner puvyqera nebhaq urer,
                          fbzrbar/fbzrguvat svaqf puvyqera
                          urer> ({anQri} <urernobhgf,> {chdch'}
                          <puvyqera>)

  {-ynU} <pna, noyr>

    {wVDbatynU} <V pna fyrrc> ({Dbat} <fyrrc>)
    {pubyrtuynU} <lbh pna frr zr> ({yrtu} <frr>)
    {ahDnj'ynU} <ur/fur pna qrfgebl hf> ({Dnj'} <qrfgebl>)


4.2.6. Glcr 6: Dhnyvsvpngvba

Yvxr Glcr 3 abha fhssvkrf, gurfr fhssvkrf fubj ubj fher gur
fcrnxre vf nobhg jung vf orvat fnvq. [[c.40]]

  {-puh'} <pyrneyl, cresrpgyl>

    {wVlnwpuh'} <V haqrefgnaq pyrneyl> ({lnw} <haqrefgnaq>)
    {onUpuh'} <ur/fur sverq (gur gbecrqb) cresrpgyl> ({onU} <sver [n
              gbecrqb]>)

  {-orw} <pregnvayl, haqbhogrqyl>

    {puVzorw} <vg vf haqbhogrqyl rzcgl> ({puVz} <or rzcgl>)
    {ahFrUorw} <ur/fur vf pregnvayl pbagebyyvat hf> ({FrU} <pba-
               geby>)

  {-ynj'} <frrzvatyl, nccneragyl>

    {puVzynj'} <vg nccrnef gb or rzcgl> ({puVz} <or rzcgl>)
    {ahFrUynj'} <ur/fur frrzf gb or pbagebyyvat hf> ({FrU} <pba-
                geby>)

  Guvf fhssvk rkcerffrf nal hapregnvagl ba gur fcrnxre'f cneg
naq znl rira or gubhtug bs nf zrnavat <V guvax> be <V fhfcrpg.>
Guhf, gur cerivbhf gjb fragraprf pbhyq or genafyngrq <V guvax
vg'f rzcgl, V fhfcrpg gung ur/fur vf pbagebyyvat hf.>


4.2.7. Glcr 7: Nfcrpg

Xyvatba qbrf abg rkcerff grafrf (cnfg, cerfrag, shgher). Gurfr
vqrnf pbzr npebff sebz pbagrkg be bgure jbeqf va gur fragrapr
(fhpu nf {jn'yrF} <gbzbeebj>). Gur ynathntr qbrf, ubjrire,
vaqvpngr nfcrpg: jurgure na npgvba vf pbzcyrgrq be abg lrg
pbzcyrgrq, naq jurgure na npgvba vf n fvatyr rirag be n
pbagvahvat bar.
  Gur nofrapr bs n Glcr 7 fhssvk hfhnyyl zrnaf gung gur npgvba
vf abg pbzcyrgrq naq vf abg pbagvahbhf (gung vf, vg vf abg bar bs
gur guvatf vaqvpngrq ol gur Glcr 7 fhssvkrf). Ireof jvgu ab
Glcr 7 fhssvk ner genafyngrq ol gur Ratyvfu fvzcyr cerfrag
grafr.

    {Qnyrtu} <lbh frr uvz/ure> ({yrtu} <frr>)
    {dnwn'} <V gryy lbh> ({wn'} <gryy>)

  Jura gur pbagrkg vf nccebcevngr, ireof jvgubhg n Glcr 7
fhssvk znl or genafyngrq ol gur Ratyvfu shgher grafr (<jvyy>), ohg
gur erny srryvat bs gur Xyvatba vf pybfre gb Ratyvfu fragraprf
fhpu nf <Jr syl gbzbeebj ng qnja,> jurer gur cerfrag-grafr
ireo ersref gb na rirag va gur shgher. [[c.41]]

  {-ch'} <cresrpgvir>

  Guvf fhssvk vaqvpngrf gung na npgvba vf pbzcyrgrq. Vg vf bsgra
genafyngrq ol gur Ratyvfu cerfrag cresrpg (<unir qbar fbzr-
guvat>).

    {Qnyrtuch'} <lbh unir frra vg> ({yrtu} <frr>)
    {iVarUch'} <V jnagrq gurz> ({arU} <jnag>)
    {dnwn'ch'} <V gbyq lbh> ({wn'} <gryy>)

  {-gn'} <nppbzcyvfurq, qbar>

  Guvf fhssvk vf fvzvyne gb {-ch',} ohg vg vf hfrq jura na npgvivgl
jnf qryvorengryl haqregnxra, gur vzcyvpngvba orvat gung fbzr-
bar frg bhg gb qb fbzrguvat naq va snpg qvq vg. Ratyvfu
genafyngvbaf fryqbz erirny gur qvfgvapgvba.

    {iVFhdgn'} <V unir npdhverq vg> ({Fhd} <trg, npdhver>)
    {yhUbUgn'} <gurl unir xvyyrq uvz/ure> ({UbU} <xvyy>)

Gur frpbaq fragrapr nobir pbhyq abg or hfrq vs gur xvyyvat
jrer gur erfhyg bs n trareny nggnpx abg vagraqrq gb xvyy n
fcrpvsvp crefba be vs gur xvyyvat jrer na nppvqrag. Va fhpu
pnfrf, {-ch'} jbhyq or hfrq:

    {yhUbUch'} <gurl unir xvyyrq uvz/ure>

  Gur zrnavat bs {-gn'} pna nyfb or vaqvpngrq flagnpgvpnyyl.
Gung vf, vafgrnq bs hfvat gur fhssvk {-gn',} n fcrpvny ireony
pbafgehpgvba pna sbyybj gur ireo juvpu vaqvpngrf gur nppbz-
cyvfurq npgvba. Guvf fcrpvny ireo vf {eVa} <or svavfurq, nppbz-
cyvfurq,> naq va guvf hfntr vg nyjnlf gnxrf gur fhssvk {-gnU}
<pbagvahbhf> (frr orybj) naq gur guveq-crefba cebabzvany
cersvk (0). Gur erfhygvat pbafgehpgvba, {eVagnU,} yvgrenyyl zrnaf
<vg pbagvahrf gb or svavfurq> be <vg erznvaf nppbzcyvfurq.> Vg vf
hfrq gb vaqvpngr gung gur npgvba qrabgrq ol gur cerprqvat ireo
vf n snvg nppbzcyv: vg vf qbar, naq vg pnaabg or haqbar.

    {yhUbU eVagnU} <gurl unir xvyyrq uvz/ure> ({UbU} <xvyy>)
    {iVwr' eVagnU} <V unir chepunfrq vg> ({wr'} <chepunfr>)

Gur Ratyvfu genafyngvbaf bs {eVagnU} naq {-gn'} ner hfhnyyl gur
fnzr. Gur abgvba bs nofbyhgr svanyvgl vzcyvrq ol {eVagnU}
fryqbz pbzrf npebff.
  Vg fubhyq or abgrq gung {eVagnU} vf fbzrgvzrf hfrq sbe [[c.42]]
qenzngvp rssrpg, rira va pnfrf jura gur npgvba pbhyq or
haqbar.

  {-gnU} <pbagvahbhf>

  Guvf fhssvk vaqvpngrf gung na npgvba vf batbvat.

    {ahtubFgnU} <vg vf nccebnpuvat hf> ({tubF} <nccebnpu>)
    {lVtubFgnU} <fgrnql ba pbhefr!, znvagnva guvf pbhefr!>
                ({tubF} <tb, nccebnpu, cebprrq ba n pbhefr>)

Obgu bs gur nobir fragraprf fhttrfg n pbagvahvat npgvivgl.
Gur zrnavat bs {-gnU} pna or frra pyrneyl ol pbzcnevat gur
sbyybjvat gjb pbzznaqf:

    {lVwha} <rkrphgr na rinfvir znarhire!>
    {lVwhagnU} <gnxr rinfvir npgvba!>

gur frpbaq, n frevrf bs rinfvir znarhiref vf gb or rkrphgrq
---gur npgvba vf gb or pbagvahbhf.

  {-yV'} <va cebterff>

  Guvf fhssvk vf fvzvyne gb {-gnU} <pbagvahbhf> va gung vg vaqvpngrf
gung na npgvivgl vf batbvat. Hayvxr {-gnU,} ubjrire, {-yV'} vzcyvrf
gung gur npgvivgl unf n xabja tbny be n qrsvavgr fgbccvat cbvag.
Va bgure jbeqf, vg fhttrfgf gung cebterff vf orvat znqr gbjneq
gung tbny.

    {pubyyV'} <vg vf trggvat pybfre>
              ({puby} <trg pybfr, pbzr arne>)

Guvf jbeq jbhyq or hfrq sbe, v.r., n zvffvyr nccebnpuvat n
gnetrg, jura vg vf xabja gung gur zvffvyr unf orra nvzrq ng
gung gnetrg. Vs n zvffvyr vf trggvat pybfre, ohg vgf vagraqrq
qrfgvangvba vf abg xabja, {pubygnU} (jvgu {-gnU} <pbagvahbhf>)

    {iVyV'yV'} <V nz genafzvggvat (gur qngn)>
               ({yV'} <genafzvg qngn gb n cynpr>)

Guvf jbeq vzcyvrf gung qngn ner va gur cebprff bs orvat
genafzvggrq, ohg gung gurer vf n svavgr nzbhag bs qngn, fb gurer
jvyy or n qrsvavgr raq gb gur genafzvffvba. Gur snpg gung gur

pbvapvqragny, fb sne nf pna or qrgrezvarq. [[c.43]]

  Gur fhssvk {-gnU} <pbagvahbhf> pna or hfrq jurgure gurer vf n
xabj tbny be abg. {-yV',} ba gur bgure unaq, pna or hfrq bayl

grecneg bs {-ch'.}

4.3. Ebiref

Gurer vf bar nqqvgvbany frg bs ireo fhssvkrf juvpu Xyvatba
tenzznevnaf pnyy {yratjV'zrl} <ebiref> (sebz {yrat} <geniry, ebnz,
ebir,> {-jV'} <guvat juvpu qbrf,> {-zrl} <cyheny>). Ebiref ner ireo
fhssvkrf juvpu qb abg unir n svkrq cbfvgvba va eryngvba gb gur
bgure fhssvkrf sbyybjvat n ireo ohg, vafgrnq, pna pbzr whfg
nobhg naljurer rkprcg sbyybjvat n Glcr 9 fhssvk. Gurve
cbfvgvba vf qrgrezvarq ol gur zrnavat vagraqrq. Gurer ner
gjb glcrf bs ebiref: gur artngvir naq gur rzcungvp.

  {-or'} <abg>

  Guvf vf gur trareny fhssvk bs artngvba, genafyngrq nf Ratyvfu
<abg.> Vg sbyybjf gur pbaprcg orvat artngrq.

    {iVyb'ynUor'} <gurl ner hfryrff gb zr, V pnaabg hfr gurz>
      {iV-}   (cersvk)  <V--gurz>
      {yb'}   (ireo)    <hfr>
      {-ynU}  (5)       <pna, noyr>
      {-or'}  (ebire)   <abg>

    {wVFnUor'} <V qba'g pner (juvpu bs frireny pbhefrf bs
               npgvba vf sbyybjrq)>
      {wV-}   (cersvk) <V>
      {FnU}   (ireo)   <pner, or pbaprearq nobhg>
      {-or'}  (ebire)  <abg>

    {dnl'or'} <vg'f abg n ceboyrz, ab ceboyrz (rkpynzngvba)>
      0       (cersvk)  <vg>
      {dnl'}  (ireo)    <or n ceboyrz, or n unffyr>
      {-or'}  (ebire)   <abg>

  Gur ebivat angher bs {-or'} vf orfg vyyhfgengrq va gur sbyybjvat
frg bs jbeqf.

    {pubUbUiVc} <lbh ner nsenvq gb xvyy zr>
    {pubUbUiVcor'} <lbh ner abg nsenvq gb xvyy zr>
    {pubUbUor'iVc} <lbh ner nsenvq gb abg xvyy zr>
      {pub-}  (cersvk)  <lbh--zr>
      {UbU}   (ireo)    <xvyy>
      {-iVc}  (2)       <nsenvq>
      {-or'}  (ebire)   <abg>

Va gur frpbaq jbeq, gur artngrq abgvba vf <nsenvq> (gung vf, <abg
nsenvq>), naq {-or'} sbyybjf {-iVc.} Va gur guveq jbeq, gur artngrq
abgvba vf <xvyy> (gung vf, <abg xvyy>), fb {-or'} sbyybjf {UbU.} [[c.47]]
  Gur fhssvk {-or'} pnaabg or hfrq jvgu vzcrengvir ireof. Sbe
vzcrengvirf, gur sbyybjvat fhssvk vf erdhverq.

  {-Db'} <qba'g!, jba'g>

  Guvf artngvir fhssvk vf hfrq va vzcrengvirf naq gb qrabgr
ershfny.

    {lVwn'Db'} <qba'g gryy uvz/ure!>
      {lV-}   (cersvk)  <vzcrengvir: lbh--uvz/ure>

  {-Un'} <haqb>

  {-dh'} <rzcungvp>

  Gur ebivat angher bs {-dh'} pna or frra va gur sbyybjvat frg:

Gur svefg jbeq nobir zvtug or hfrq nsgre na rarzl puny-
yratrq gur oenirel bs gur fcrnxre. Gur frpbaq zvtug or
sbyybjrq ol na rkcynangvba fhpu nf, "Jr ner abg jvyyvat gb xvyy
lbh orpnhfr jr erdhver lbhe freivprf." Gur guveq jbeq jbhyq
or hfrq gb rzcunfvmr xvyyvat, nf bccbfrq gb fbzr bgure sbez
bs chavfuzrag.
  Gur ebire {-dh'} nyfb sbyybjf ireof jura gurl ner hfrq
nqwrpgvinyyl (frpgvba 4.4).


4.4 Nqwrpgvirf [[4.4:=4.4.]]

Gurer ner ab nqwrpgvirf nf fhpu va Xyvatba. Gubfr abgvbaf
rkcerffrq nf nqwrpgvirf va Ratyvfu (fhpu nf <ovt, gverq>) ner
rkcerffrq ol ireof va Xyvatba (<or ovt, or gverq>). N ireo
rkcerffvat n fgngr be dhnyvgl pna or hfrq vzzrqvngryl sbyybj-
vat n abha gb zbqvsl gung abha.

    {chd Qbl'} <gverq puvyq>
    {chd} <puvyq>
    {Qbl'} <or gverq>

    {Qhwzrl gVa} <ovt fuvcf>
    {Qhwzrl} <fuvcf, irffryf>
    {gVa} <or ovt>

  Gur ebire {-dh'} <rzcungvp> (frpgvba 4.3) znl sbyybj ireof
shapgvbavat nqwrpgvinyyl. Va guvf hfntr, vg vf hfhnyyl genafyngrq
<irel.>

    {Qhwzrl gVadh'} <irel ovt fuvcf> [[c.50]]
    {jnaV' enzdh'} <n irel havzcbegnag rirag>
    {jnaV'} <rirag, bppheerapr>
    {enz} <or gevivny, havzcbegnag>

  Vs n Glcr 5 abha fhssvk vf hfrq (frpgvba 3.3.5), vg sbyybjf gur
ireo, juvpu, jura hfrq gb zbqvsl gur abha va guvf jnl, pna
unir ab bgure fhssvk rkprcg gur ebire {-dh'} <rzcungvp.> Gur Glcr
5 abha fhssvk sbyybjf {-dh'.}

    {irat gVaQnd} <va gur ovt pvgl>
    {irat} <pvgl>
    {gVa} <or ovt>
    {-Qnd} <ybpngvir>

    {irat gVadh'Qnd} <va gur irel ovt pvgl> [[c.51]]


5. BGURE XVAQF BS JBEQF

Ol sne gur ohyx bs Xyvatba jbeqf ner abhaf naq ireof. Gurer
ner n srj bguref juvpu, cebonoyl nf na rkcrqvrag, Xyvatba
tenzznevnaf yhzc gbtrgure va n tebhc pnyyrq {puhizrl}
<yrsgbiref.> Vg vf cbffvoyr gb pynffvsl gur {puhizrl} fbzr-
jung.


5.1. Cebabhaf

Va nqqvgvba gb cbffrffvir fhssvkrf sbe abhaf (frpgvba 3.3.4) naq
cebabzvany cersvkrf sbe ireof (frpgvba 4.1), gurer vf n frg bs
avar cebabhaf juvpu ner vaqrcraqrag jbeqf. [[avar:=gra]]

    {wVU} <V, zr>             {znU} <jr, hf>
    {fbU} <lbh>               {gyuVU} <lbh (cyheny)> [[fbU:=FbU]]
    {tunU} <ur/fur, uvz/ure>  {punU} <gurl, gurz>
    {'bU} <vg>                {oVU} <gurl, gurz>
    {'r'} <gung>
    {arg} <gung>

  Gur cebabha {punU} <gurl> vf hfrq jura vg ersref gb n tebhc bs
orvatf pncnoyr bs hfvat ynathntr; bgurejvfr, {oVU} <gurl> vf hfrq.
Gur cebabhaf {'r'} naq {arg} ner hfrq bayl va fcrpvny fragrapr
pbafgehpgvbaf (frr frpgvba 6.2.5).
  Gurer vf ab tenzzngvpny traqre va Xyvatba. Guveq-crefba [[c.52]]
fvathyne cebabhaf pna or genafyngrq <ur> be <fur> nf pbagrkg
qvpgngrf.
  Cebabhaf znl or hfrq nf abhaf, ohg bayl sbe rzcunfvf be
nqqrq pynevgl. Gurl ner abg erdhverq. Guhf, gur sbyybjvat frgf
bs fragraprf ner nyy tenzzngvpnyyl pbeerpg.

    {lnF iVyrtu wVU} <V frr gur bssvpref.>
    {lnF iVyrtu}

    {wVU zhyrtu lnF} <Gur bssvpre frrf zr.>
    {zhyrtu lnF}

    {tunU iVyrtu wVU} <V frr uvz/ure.>
    {tunU iVyrtu}
    {iVyrtu wVU}
    {iVyrtu}
    ({lnF} <bssvpre,> {iVyrtu} <V frr uvz/ure,> {zhyrtu} <ur/fur frrf zr>)

  Gur svany gjb fragraprf ({iVyrtu wVU, iVyrtu}) ner va snpg
nzovthbhf. Gurl pbhyq rdhnyyl jryy zrna <V frr gurz.> (Gur
ireo cersvk {iV-} vf rvgure <V--uvz/ure> be <V--gurz.>) Vs pbagrkg qbrf
abg znxr vg pyrne juvpu zrnavat vf vagraqrq, cebabhaf pna or
hfrq:

    {tunU iVyrtu} <V frr uvz/ure.>
    {punU iVyrtu} <V frr gurz.>

  Cebabhaf ner abg hfrq va cbffrffvir pbafgehpgvbaf va gur
jnl abhaf ner; vafgrnq, gur frg bs cbffrffvir abha fhssvkrf vf
hfrq (frpgvba 3.3.4).
  Svanyyl, cebabhaf pna or hfrq nf ireof, va gur frafr bs "V
nz," rgp. (Frr frpgvba 6.3).


5.2. Ahzoref

Xyvatba bevtvanyyl unq n greanel ahzore flfgrz; gung vf, bar
onfrq ba guerr. Pbhagvat cebprrqrq nf sbyybjf: 1, 2, 3; 3+1,
3+2, 3+3; 2×3+1, 2×3+2, 2×3+3; 3×3+1, 3×3+2,
3×3+3; naq gura vg tbg pbzcyvpngrq. Va nppbeqnapr jvgu
gur zber npprcgrq cenpgvpr, gur Xyvatba Rzcver fbzrgvzr
onpx nqbcgrq n qrpvzny ahzore flfgrz, bar onfrq ba gra. [[c.53]]
Gubhtu ab bar xabjf sbe fher, vg vf yvxryl gung guvf punatr
jnf znqr zber bhg bs pbaprea sbe haqrefgnaqvat gur fpvra-
gvsvp qngn bs bgure pvivyvmngvbaf guna bhg bs n fcvevg bs pbbcre-
ngvba.
  Gur Xyvatba ahzoref ner:

    1 {jn'}    6 {wni}
    2 {pun'}   7 {Fbpu}
    3 {jrw}    8 {pubetu}
    4 {ybF}    9 {Uhg}
    5 {intu}   10 {jn'znU}

  Uvture ahzoref ner sbezrq ol nqqvat fcrpvny ahzore- [[xrrc ulcura]]
sbezvat ryrzragf gb gur onfvp frg bs ahzoref (1--9). Guhf,
{jn'znU} <gra> pbafvfgf bs {jn'} <bar> cyhf gur ahzore-sbezvat
ryrzrag sbe <gra,> {znU.} Pbhagvat pbagvahrf nf sbyybjf:

    11  {jn'znU jn'}   (gung vf, <gra naq bar>)
    12  {jn'znU pun'}  (gung vf, <gra naq gjb>)
    rgp.

  Uvture ahzoref ner onfrq ba {znU} <gra,> {ingyu} <uhaqerq,> naq
{FnQ} be {FnaVQ} <gubhfnaq.> Obgu {FnQ} naq {FnaVQ} ner rdhnyyl
pbeerpg sbe <gubhfnaq,> naq obgu ner hfrq jvgu ebhtuyl rdhny
serdhrapl. Vg vf abg xabja jul guvf ahzore nybar unf gjb
inevnagf.

    20     {pun'znU}                 (gung vf, <gjb graf>)
    30     {jrwznU}                  (gung vf, <guerr graf>)
    rgp.

    100    {jn'ingyu}                (gung vf, <bar uhaqerq>)
    200    {pun'ingyu}               (gung vf, <gjb uhaqerqf>)
    rgp.

    1,000  {jn'FnQ} be {jn'FnaVQ}    (gung vf, <bar gubhfnaq>)
    2,000  {pun'FnQ} be {pun'FnaVQ}  (gung vf, <gjb gubhfnaqf>)
    rgp.

  Ahzoref ner pbzovarq nf va Ratyvfu:

    5,347 {intuFnq jrwingyu ybFznU Fbpu} be [[intuFnq:=intuFnQ]] [[c.54]]
    {intuFnaVQ jrwingyu ybFznU Fbpu}
    604 {wniingyu ybF}
    31 {jrwznU jn'}

  Fbzr bs gur ahzore-sbezvat ryrzragf sbe uvture ahzoref
ner:

    gra gubhfnaq      {argyu}
    uhaqerq gubhfnaq  {oVc}
    zvyyvba           {'hl'}

  Mreb vf {cntu.}

  Ahzoref ner hfrq nf abhaf. Nf fhpu, gurl znl fgnaq nybar
nf fhowrpgf be bowrpgf be gurl znl zbqvsl nabgure abha.

    {zhyrtu pun'} <Gjb (bs gurz) frr zr.>
                  ({zhyrtu} <gurl frr zr,> {pun'} <gjb>)

    {jn' lVUbU} <Xvyy bar (bs gurz)!>
                ({jn'} <bar,> {lVUbU} <xvyy uvz/ure!>)

Gur cerprqvat fragrapr vf tenzzngvpnyyl pbeerpg rira jvgubhg
gur {jn'} orpnhfr gur cersvk {lV-} vaqvpngrf n fvathyne bowrpg. Gur
{jn',} gurersber, vf hfrq sbe rzcunfvf bayl.
  Ahzoref hfrq nf zbqvsvref cerprqr gur abha gurl zbqvsl.

    {ybF chdch'} be {ybF chd} <sbhe puvyqera>
    {intuznU lhDzrl} be {intuznU lhD} <svsgl cynargf>

Gur cyheny fhssvkrf ({-ch', -zrl}) ner abg arprffnel jura n
ahzore vf hfrq.
  Jura n ahzore vf hfrq sbe ahzorevat, nf bccbfrq gb
pbhagvat, vg sbyybjf gur abha. Pbzcner:

    {QhF jn'} <gbecrqb ghor ahzore 1>
    {jn' QhF} <bar gbecrqb ghor>

  Beqvany ahzoref (<svefg, frpbaq,> rgp.) ner sbezrq ol nqqvat
{-QVpu} gb gur ahzoref.

    {jn'QVpu} <svefg>
    {pun'QVpu} <frpbaq>
    {UhgQVpu} <avagu>

Beqvany ahzoref sbyybj gur abha.

    {zro pun'QVpu} <frpbaq thrfg> [[c.55]]

  Nqqvat {-ybtu} gb n ahzore tvirf gur abgvba bs ercrgvgvbaf.

    {jn'ybtu} <bapr>
    {pun'ybtu} <gjvpr>
    {Uhgybtu} <avar gvzrf>

Gurfr ahzoref shapgvba va gur fragrapr nf nqireovnyf (frpgvba
5.4).


5.3. Pbawhapgvbaf

Pbawhapgvbaf ner bs gjb glcrf: gubfr gung wbva abhaf gbtrgure
naq gubfr gung wbva fragraprf gbtrgure. Gur zrnavatf bs gur
gjb glcrf bs pbawhapgvbaf, ubjrire, ner gur fnzr:

    WBVAVAT ABHAF  WBVAVAT FRAGRAPRF
      {wr}           {'rw}            <naq>
      {wbd}          {dbw}            <naq/be>
      {tunc}         {cntu}           <rvgure/be>

  Gur pbawhapgvbaf wbvavat abhaf pbzr nsgre gur svany abha.

    {QrF 'hF wr} <na nez naq n yrt>
    {QrF 'hF wbd} <na nez be n yrt be obgu>
    {QrF 'hF tunc} <rvgure na nez be n yrt (ohg abg obgu)>

  Gur abha pbawhapgvba {wr} unf na nqqvgvbany shapgvba: jura vg
sbyybjf n ireo, vg zrnaf <nyfb, gbb.>

    {dnyrtuch' wr} <V nyfb fnj lbh, V fnj lbh gbb>

  Nf va Ratyvfu, gur zrnavat bs fhpu fragraprf vf nzovthbhf:
<V naq bguref fnj lbh> be <V fnj lbh naq bguref.> Gur rknpg
zrnavat vf qrgrezvarq ol pbagrkg.
  Va nqqvgvba gb gur guerr yvfgrq nobir, gurer vf bar bgure
fragrapr pbawhapgvba:

    {'npu} <ohg, arireguryrff, ubjrire, rira fb>

Guvf jbeq vf fbzrgvzrf fubegrarq gb {'n.}
  Gur pbawhapgvbaf wbvavat fragraprf bpphe orgjrra gur
fragraprf gurl wbva. Sbe vyyhfgengvbaf, frr frpgvba 6.2.1.


5.4. Nqireovnyf

Gurfr jbeqf hfhnyyl pbzr ng gur ortvaavat bs n fragrapr naq

  Rknzcyrf:

    {obat lnF iVUbUch'} <V nppvqragnyyl xvyyrq gur bssvpre.>
                        ({lnF} <bssvpre,> {iVUbUch'} <V xvyyrq
                        uvz/ure>)
    {ongyu Qndnjyh'gnU} <Lbh jvyy or erzrzorerq jvgu ubabe.>

                        erzrzore lbh>)

  Bar jbeq svgf fbzrjung njxjneqyl vagb guvf pngrtbel:

  {arU} <bayl, zreryl, whfg>

Hayvxr gur bgure nqireovnyf, vg sbyybjf gur ireo juvpu vg

    {dnzn' iVdVcch' arU} <V zreryl uvg gur cevfbare.>

Gur hfr bs {arU} va gur cerprqvat fragrapr vzcyvrf gung gur fuvc

5.5 Rkpynzngvbaf [[5.5:=5.5.]]

    {gbU} <Jryy! Fb!>
    {jrwchU} <Punezvat.> (hfrq bayl vebavpnyyl)

  {UVwn'} naq {UVFynU} <lrf> frrz gb or hfrq vagrepunatrnoyl.
  {FhU, Fh',} naq {'rU} nyy zrna gung gur fcrnxre vf nobhg gb tvir
n pbzznaq. Gurl ner pbzcnenoyr gb gur "Ernql!" ng gur
ortvaavat bs n enpr: "Ernql! Frg! Tb!" {FhU} naq {Fh',} ohg abg
{'rU,} pna nyfb or hfrq gb vaqvpngr gung gur fcrnxre vf ernql gb

phefrf. Bayl guerr fhpu phefrf unir orra abgrq gb qngr.
