5.6. Anzrf naq nqqerff

Xyvatba anzrf ner serdhragyl zvfcebabhaprq ol aba- [[xrrc ulcura]]
Xyvatbaf. Shegurezber, jura jevggra va gur jevgvat flfgrzf
bs bgure ynathntrf, gurl hfhnyyl raq hc jvgu fcryyvatf juvpu
bayl fhttrfg gurve gehr cebahapvngvba. Sbe rknzcyr, gur
Xyvatba fbhaq {gyu} ng gur ortvaavat bs n jbeq vf nyzbfg nyjnlf
jevggra <xy> ol Ratyvfu fcrnxref, cerfhznoyl orpnhfr gur fbhaq
<gy> pnaabg bpphe ng gur ortvaavat bs na Ratyvfu jbeq. Fvzvyneyl,
Xyvatba {D} vf bsgra eraqrerq <xe,> naq Xyvatba {d} nyjnlf pbzrf
bhg <x.>
  Gur sbyybjvat vf n yvfg bs n srj Xyvatba anzrf nybat jvgu
gurve hfhny Ratyvfu fcryyvatf.

    {znen}     <Znen>
    {zngyu}    <Znygm>
    {drat}     <Xnat>
    {drlyVF}   <Xnuyrff>
    {dbybgyu}  <Xbybgu>
    {dbe}      <Xbe>
    {dberD}    <Xbenk>
    {DnF}      <Xenf>
    {Dry}      <Xeryy>
    {Dhtu}     <Xehtr>
    {gbetu}    <Gbet>
    {inyDVF}   <Inyxevf>

  Anzrf znl or hfrq va qverpg nqqerff (gung vf, pnyyvat
fbzrobql ol anzr) ng gur ortvaavat be raq bs gur fragrapr.
Bgure jbeqf va qverpg nqqerff (fhpu nf {dnU} <fve,> {wbUjV'} <zl
ybeq>) ner hfrq fvzvyneyl.

    {gbetu UVtubF} <Gbet, pbzr urer!> ({UVtubF} <ceb-
                   prrq gbjneq zr!>)

    {yh' dnU} <Lrf, fve!> [[c.59]]


6. FLAGNK

Nf va nal ynathntr, Xyvatba fragraprf enatr sebz gur irel
fvzcyr naq fgenvtugsbejneq gb gur irel pbzcyrk naq pbaib-
yhgrq. Jung sbyybjf urer ner gur zrer onfvpf bs Xyvatba
fragrapr fgehpgher. Guvf vasbezngvba fubhyq cebivqr n tbbq
sbhaqngvba fb gung fghqragf bs Xyvatba pna pbairefr cebcreyl,
gubhtu abg rybdhragyl, juvyr yrneavat zber nobhg gur yna-
thntr.


6.1. Onfvp fragraprf

Gur onfvp fgehpgher bs n Xyvatba fragrapr vf:

    BOWRPG--IREO--FHOWRPG

Guvf gur erirefr bs gur beqre va Ratyvfu, fb pner fubhyq or
gnxra gb nibvq vagrecergvat fragraprf onpxjneq. Gur fhowrpg
vf gur crefba be guvat qbvat gur npgvba qrfpevorq ol gur ireo;
Gur bowrpg vf gur erpvcvrag bs gung npgvba.
  Gur vzcbegnapr bs jbeq beqre pna or frra ol pbzcnevat
gur sbyybjvat fragraprf.

    {chd yrtu lnF} <Gur bssvpre frrf gur puvyq.>
    {lnF yrtu chd} <Gur puvyq frrf gur bssvpre.>

Va obgu fragraprf, gur jbeqf ner vqragvpny: {chd} <puvyq,> {yrtu} [[c.60]]
<ur/fur frrf uvz/ure,> {lnF} <bssvpre.> Gur bayl jnl gb xabj jub vf
frrvat jubz vf ol gur beqre bs gur jbeqf va gur fragrapr. Gur
ireo {yrtu} vf cerprqrq ol gur cersvk 0 <ur/fur--uvz/ure.>
  Jura gur fhowrpg naq/be bowrpg vf svefg be frpbaq crefba,
gur cersvk ba gur ireo zhfg or gur cebcre bar.

    {chd iVyrtu wVU} <V frr gur puvyq.>
                     ({iVyrtu} <V frr uvz/ure>)
    {wVU zhyrtu chd} <Gur puvyq frrf zr.>
                     ({zhyrtu} <ur/fur frrf zr>)

Npghnyyl, gur svefg- naq frpbaq-crefba cebabhaf ner fryqbz
hfrq va fragraprf bs guvf glcr (gubhtu gurl pna, nf urer, or
hfrq sbe rzcunfvf), fb gur sbyybjvat fragraprf vyyhfgengr zber
pbzzbayl bppheevat fragrapr glcrf.

    {chd iVyrtu} <V frr gur puvyq.>
    {zhyrtu chd} <Gur puvyq frrf zr.>

  Vzcrengvir fragraprf (pbzznaqf) sbyybj gur fnzr ehyrf.

    {Fb'jV' lVpuh'} <Ratntr gur pybnxvat qrivpr!>
                    ({Fb'jV'} <pybnxvat qrivpr,>
                    {lVpuh'} <ratntr vg!>)
    {QbF lVohF} <Pbapragengr ba gur gnetrg!>
                ({QbF} <gnetrg,> {lVohF} <pbapragengr ba vg!>)
    {lnFch' gVUbU} <Xvyy gur bssvpref!>
                   ({lnFch'} <bssvpref,> {gVUbU} <xvyy gurz!>)

  Nal abha va gur fragrapr vaqvpngvat fbzrguvat bgure guna
fhowrpg be bowrpg pbzrf svefg, orsber gur bowrpg abha. Fhpu
abhaf hfhnyyl raq va n Glcr 5 abha fhssvk (frpgvba 3.3.5).

    {cn'Qnd lnF iVyrtuch'} <V fnj gur bssvpre va gur ebbz.>
                           ({cn'Qnd} <va gur ebbz,>
                           {lnF} <bssvpre,> {iVyrtuch'} <V fnj uvz/
                           ure>)

  Bgure rknzcyrf bs guvf pbafgehpgvba ner tvira va frpgvba
3.3.5.


6.2. Pbzcyrk fragraprf

N srj bs gur zber pbzzba glcrf bs zber rynobengr Xyvatba
fragraprf jvyy or vyyhfgengrq. [[c.61]]


6.2.1. Pbzcbhaq fragraprf

Gjb fragraprf znl or wbvarq gbtrgure gb sbez n ybatre
pbzcbhaq fragrapr. Obgu fragraprf zhfg or noyr gb fgnaq
nybar nf cebcreyl sbezrq fragraprf. Jura pbzovarq, gurl
fvzcyl pbzr bar nsgre gur bgure, wbvarq ol n pbawhapgvba (frr
frpgvba 5.3).

    {wVFbcgnU 'rw DbatgnU} <V nz rngvat, naq ur/fur vf
                           fyrrcvat.>
    {wVFbcgnU 'npu DbatgnU} <V nz rngvat, ohg ur/fur vf
                            fyrrcvat.>

    {oVFbcgnU dbw oVgyuhgyugnU} <Lbh ner rngvat naq/be
                                lbh ner qevaxvat.>
    {oVFbcgnU cntu oVgyuhgyugnU} <Lbh ner rvgure rngvat be ryfr
                                 lbh ner qevaxvat.>

  Jura gur fhowrpg bs obgu bs gur wbvarq fragraprf vf
gur fnzr, gur Ratyvfu genafyngvba znl or erqhprq gb n yrff
pubccl sbez, ohg Xyvatba qbrf abg nyybj guvf fubegravat.
Gur cebabzvany cersvk zhfg or hfrq jvgu obgu ireof.
Guhf, gur svany gjb fragraprf nobir znl or genafyngrq
<Lbh ner rngvat naq/be qevaxvat; Lbh ner rvgure rngvat be
qevaxvat.>
  Jura n abha (nf bccbfrq gb fvzcyl n ireony cersvk)
vaqvpngrf fhowrpg naq/be bowrpg, gurer ner fbzr bcgvbaf va
Xyvatba. Va vgf shyyrfg sbez, n Xyvatba fragrapr ercrngf gur
abha:

    {lnF yrtu chd 'rw lnF dVc chd}
      ({lnF} <bssvpre,> {chd} <puvyq,> {yrtu} <ur/fur frrf
      uvz/ure,> {dVc} <ur/fur uvgf uvz/ure>)
      <Gur puvyq frrf gur bssvpre naq gur puvyq uvgf
      gur bssvpre.>
        be
      <Gur puvyq frrf gur bssvpre naq uvgf gur bssvpre.>
        be
      <Gur puvyq frrf naq uvgf gur bssvpre.>

Vg vf cbffvoyr, ubjrire, gb hfr cebabhaf engure guna abhaf va
gur frpbaq bs gur wbvarq fragraprf. [[c.62]]

    {lnF yrtu chd 'rw tunU dVc tunU} ({tunU} <ur/fur>)
      <Gur puvyq frrf gur bssvpre naq ur/fur uvgf uvz/ure.>
        be
      <Gur puvyq frrf gur bssvpre naq uvgf uvz/ure.>

Vs gur pbagrkg vf pyrne, rira gur cebabha znl or yrsg bhg.

    {lnF iVyrtu 'rw iVdVc} ({iV-} <V--uvz/ure>)
      <V frr gur bssvpre naq V uvg uvz/ure.>
        be
      <V frr gur bssvpre naq uvg uvz/ure.>
        be
      <V frr naq uvg gur bssvpre.>


6.2.2. Fhobeqvangr pynhfrf

Xyvatba ireof raqvat va Glcr 9 fhssvkrf (bgure guna {-'n'}
<vagreebtngvir> naq {-jV'} <bar jub qbrf, bar juvpu qbrf>) nyjnlf
bpphe va fragraprf jvgu nabgure ireo. Urapr, gurl ner ireof
va fhobeqvangr pynhfrf.

       {pun lVonU dnen'QV'}
    be {dnen'QV' pun lVonU} <Sver gur gbecrqbrf ng zl pbz-
                            znaq!>

  Gur gjb cnegf bs guvf fragrapr ner {pun lVonU} <sver gur
gbecrqbrf!> naq {dnen'QV'} <jura V pbzznaq lbh> be <nf fbba nf V
pbzznaq lbh.> {-QV'} vf n Glcr 9 fhssvk zrnavat <nf fbba nf,
jura,> fb {dnen'QV'} zhfg bpphe nf cneg bs n ynetre fragrapr.
Abgr gung gur beqre bs gur gjb cnegf bs gur fragrapr vf
inevnoyr.
  N srj shegure rknzcyrf fubhyq znxr gur hfr bs fhobeqvangr
pynhfrf pyrne.

       {oVwngyuUn'puhtu dnUbU}
    be {dnUbU oVwngyuUn'puhtu} <Vs lbh fnl gur jebat guvat,
                               V jvyy xvyy lbh.>
                               ({oVwngyuUn'puhtu} <vs lbh
                               zvffcrnx,> {dnUbU} <V xvyy
                               lbh>)

Abgr gung nygubhtu gur Ratyvfu genafyngvba hfrf gur jbeq <jvyy,>
gurer vf ab znexre sbe shgher va Xyvatba. Gur hafhssvkrq ireo
{UbU} <xvyy> vf arhgeny nf gb gvzr: fvapr gur crefba orvat [[c.63]]
nqqerffrq vf orvat tvira n punapr gb fcrnx, gung crefba zhfg
fgvyy or nyvir. Guhf, gur xvyyvat zhfg gnxr cynpr va gur shgher.

       {FhgyugnUiVF punU QVUVich'}
    be {QVUVich' FhgyugnUiVF punU} <Juvyr gurl jrer
                                   artbgvngvat jr
                                   nggnpxrq gurz.>
                                   ({FhgyugnUiVF} <juvyr
                                   gurl ner artbgvngvat,>
                                   {punU} <gurl,> {QVUVich'}
                                   <jr nggnpxrq gurz>)

Gur abgvba bs <jrer artbgvngvat,> engure guna <ner artbgvngvat,>
pbzrf sebz gur fhssvk {-ch'} <cresrpgvir> nggnpurq gb gur ireo {UVi}
<nggnpx.> N genafyngvba fhpu nf <Juvyr gurl ner artbgvngvat jr
nggnpxrq gurz> znxrf yvggyr frafr va Ratyvfu naq zvfercerfragf
gur zrnavat bs gur Xyvatba fragrapr.


6.2.3. Eryngvir pynhfrf

Eryngvir pynhfrf ner genafyngrq vagb Ratyvfu nf cuenfrf ortva-
avat jvgu <jub, juvpu, jurer,> naq, zbfg pbzzbayl, <gung.> Yvxr
nqwrpgvirf, gurl qrfpevor abhaf: <gur qbt juvpu vf ehaavat, gur
png gung vf fyrrcvat, gur puvyq jub vf cynlvat, gur erfgnhenag
jurer jr ngr.> Gur abha zbqvsvrq ol n eryngvir pynhfr vf gur
urnq abha.
  Va Xyvatba, gur ireo va gur eryngvir pynhfr raqf jvgu gur
Glcr 9 fhssvk {-obtu,} juvpu jvyy, sbe pbairavrapr, or genafyngrq
<juvpu.>
  Jurgure gur urnq abha sbyybjf be cerprqrf gur eryngvir
pynhfr qrcraqf ba vgf eryngvbafuvc gb gung pynhfr. Pbzcner gur
sbyybjvat:

    {dVcch'obtu lnF} <bssvpre jub uvg uvz/ure>
    {lnF dVcch'obtu} <bssvpre jubz ur/fur uvg>

Va obgu cuenfrf, gur eryngvir pynhfr vf {dVcch'obtu} ({dVc} <uvg,>
{-ch'} <cresrpgvir,> {-obtu} <juvpu>), naq gur urnq abha vf {lnF}
<bssvpre.> Va gur svefg cuenfr, {lnF} vf gur fhowrpg bs gur ireo {dVc}
(gur bssvpre vf qbvat gur uvggvat), fb vg sbyybjf {dVcch'obtu,} whfg
nf nyy fhowrpgf sbyybj gur ireo. Va gur frpbaq cuenfr, {lnF} vf gur [[c.64]]
bowrpg (gur bssvpre vf trggvat uvg), fb vg cerprqrf {dVcch'obtu,}
whfg nf nyy bowrpgf cerprqr gur ireo.
  Gur jubyr pbafgehpgvba (eryngvir pynhfr cyhf urnq abha), nf
n havg, vf hfrq va n fragrapr nf n abha. Nppbeqvatyl, guvf
pbafgehpgvba sbyybjf be cerprqrf gur ireo bs gur fragrapr,
qrcraqvat ba jurgure vg vf gur fhowrpg be bowrpg.

    {dVcch'obtu lnF iVyrtu} <V frr gur bssvpre jub uvg
                            uvz/ure.>

Gur ragver eryngvir pbafgehpgvba {dVcch'obtu lnF} <bssvpre jub
uvg uvz/ure> vf gur bowrpg bs gur ireo {iVyrtu} <V frr uvz/ure,> fb vg
cerprqrf gur ireo.

    {zhyrtu dVcch'obtu lnF} <Gur bssvpre jub uvg uvz/ure
                            frrf zr.>

Urer, {dVcch'obtu lnF} vf gur fhowrpg bs gur ireo {zhyrtu} <ur/fur
frrf zr,> fb vg sbyybjf gur ireo.
  Guvf cnggrea vf nyfb sbyybjrq jura gur urnq abha vf gur
bowrpg bs gur ireo va gur eryngvir pynhfr, fhpu nf {lnF
dVcch'obtu} <bssvpre jubz ur/fur uvg.>

    {lnF dVcch'obtu iVyrtu} <V frr gur bssvpre jubz ur/fur
                            uvg.>
    {zhyrtu lnF dVcch'obtu} <Gur bssvpre jubz ur/fur uvg
                            frrf zr.>

  Va gur Ratyvfu genafyngvba, gur eryngvir cebabhaf (<gung,
juvpu,> rgp.) znl bsgra or bzvggrq: <V frr gur bssvpre ur/fur uvg,
gur bssvpre ur/fur uvg frrf zr.> Va Xyvatba, ubjrire, {-obtu} vf
znaqngbel.


6.2.4. Checbfr pynhfrf

Vs na npgvba vf orvat qbar va beqre gb nppbzcyvfu fbzrguvat,
be sbe gur checbfr bs nppbzcyvfuvat fbzrguvat, gur ireo
qrfpevovat jung vf gb or nppbzcyvfurq raqf jvgu gur Glcr 9
fhssvk {-zrU,} juvpu znl or genafyngrq <sbe, sbe gur checbfr bs,
va beqre gb.> Gur checbfr pynhfr nyjnlf cerprqrf gur abha be
ireo jubfr checbfr vg vf qrfpevovat.

    {wn'puhdzrU ebwUbz arU wntuyn'} <Gur rarzl pbzznaqre [[wntuyn':=wntu yn']]
                                    jvfurf n gehpr (va beqre)
                                    gb pbasre.> [[c.65]]

Gur cuenfr {wn'puhdzrU ebwUbz} <n gehpr (va beqre) gb pbasre> vf
gur bowrpg bs gur ireo {arU} <ur/fur jnagf vg;> gur fhowrpg vf
{wntuyn'} <rarzl pbzznaqre.> Gur bowrpg vf n abha {ebwUbz} <gehpr> [[wntuyn':=wntu yn']]
cerprqrq ol gur checbfr pynhfr {wn'puhdzrU} <sbe gur checbfr
bs pbasreevat> be <va beqre gb pbasre.> (Gur ireo vf znqr hc bs {wn'}
<gryy,> {-puhd} <rnpu bgure;> guhf, <pbasre> vf <gryy rnpu bgure.>)

    {wntu yhUbUzrU wntu yharwgnU} <Gurl ner frnepuvat sbe
                                  gur rarzl va beqre gb
                                  xvyy uvz/ure.>

Urer gur checbfr pynhfr vf {wntu yhUbUzrU} <va beqre sbe gurz
gb xvyy gur rarzl,> juvpu vf znqr hc bs gur bowrpg abha {wntu}
<rarzl> cerprqvat gur ireo {yhUbUzrU} <va beqre sbe gurz gb xvyy
uvz/ure> ({yh-} <gurl--uvz/ure,> {UbU} <xvyy,> {-zrU} <sbe>). Vg qrfpevorf
gur checbfr bs gur ireo {yharwgnU} <gurl ner frnepuvat sbe
uvz/ure> ({yh-} <gurl--uvz/ure,> {arw} <frrx, frnepu sbe,> {-gnU} <pbagvah-
bhf>). Abgr gung, whfg nf va pbzcbhaq fragraprf, gur bowrpg
abha {wntu} <rarzl> bpphef orsber rnpu ireo sbe juvpu vg vf gur
bowrpg. Guhf, fbzrjung zber yvgrenyyl, gur fragrapr znl or
genafyngrq <Va beqre gb xvyy gur rarzl, gurl ner frnepuvat sbe gur
rarzl.>
  Shegurezber, whfg nf va pbzcbhaq fragraprf, gur frpbaq bs
gjb vqragvpny abhaf znl or ercynprq ol n cebabha be, vs gur
pbagrkg, vf pyrne, yrsg bhg nygbtrgure.

    {wntu yhUbUzrU tunU yharwgnU}
    {wntu yhUbUzrU yharwgnU} <Gurl ner frnepuvat sbe gur
                             rarzl va beqre gb xvyy
                             uvz/ure.>


6.2.5. Fragraprf nf bowrpgf

Xyvatba unf gjb fcrpvny cebabhaf, {'r'} naq {arg,} juvpu ersre gb
gur cerivbhf fragrapr nf n jubyr. Gurl ner hfrq cevznevyl,
gubhtu abg rkpyhfviryl, jvgu ireof bs guvaxvat be bofreingvba
(fhpu nf <xabj, frr>). Gurl ner nyjnlf gerngrq nf gur bowrpg
bs gur ireo, naq gur ireo nyjnlf gnxrf n cersvk vaqvpngvat
n guveq-crefba fvathyne bowrpg. Jung vf n fvatyr fragrapr
va Ratyvfu vf bsgra gjb fragraprf va Xyvatba. {arg} vf hfrq
bayl haqre fcrpvny pvephzfgnaprf (frr cntr 66), ohg {'r'} vf
pbzzba. Frireny rknzcyrf fubhyq znxr gur hfr bs {'r'}
pyrne. [[c.66]]

    {dnzn'ch' QVUbU 'r' yhFbi} <Gurl xabj jr xvyy cevfbaref.>

Guvf fragrapr vf npghnyyl gjb: (1) {dnzn'ch' QVUbU} <Jr xvyy
cevfbaref> ({dnzn'ch'} <cevfbaref,> {QVUbU} <jr xvyy gurz>); (2) {'r'
yhFbi} <Gurl xabj gung> ({'r'} <gung,> {yhFbi} <gurl xabj vg>). Gur
cebabha {'r'} ersref gb gur cerivbhf fragrapr, <Jr xvyy cevfbaref.>

    {lnF dVcch' 'r' iVyrtu} <V fnj uvz/ure uvg gur bssvpref.>

Gur gjb fragraprf urer ner: (1) {lnF dVcch'} <Ur/fur uvg gur
bssvpre;> (2) {'r' iVyrtu} <V frr gung> ({iVyrtu} <V frr vg>). Gur pbafgehp-
gvba zvtug rdhnyyl jryy or genafyngrq nf <V fnj gung ur/fur uvg
gur bssvpre.> Abgr gung gur ireo va gur frpbaq fragrapr, {iVyrtu} <V
frr vg,> vf arhgeny nf gb gvzr. Gur cnfg grafr bs gur genafyngvba
<(V fnj...)> pbzrf sebz gur ireo va gur svefg fragrapr, {dVcch'}
<ur/fur uvg uvz/ure> ({-ch'} <cresrpgvir>). Va pbzcyrk fragraprf bs
guvf glcr, gur frpbaq ireo arire gnxrf na nfcrpg fhssvk (frpgvba
4.2.7).

  Jura gur ireo bs gur frpbaq fragrapr unf n guveq-crefba
fhowrpg (gung vf, gur cebabzvany cersvk vf 0) ohg gur vagraqrq
zrnavat vf <bar> be <fbzrbar,> engure guna <ur, fur, vg,> be <gurl,> {arg}
vf hfrq vafgrnq bs {'r'.}

    {dnzn'ch' QVUbU arg Fbi} <Bar xabjf jr xvyy  cevfbaref.>

Nf nobir, gur svefg fragrapr urer vf {dnzn'ch' QVUbU} <Jr xvyy
cevfbaref.> Gur frpbaq fragrapr vf {arg Fbi} <Bar xabjf gung.>
Gur shyy pbafgehpgvba vzcyvrf gung vg vf pbzzba xabjyrqtr
gung gur tebhc gb juvpu gur fcrnxre orybatf xvyyf cevfbaref.

    {Dh'inQ yV' arg gh'orw} <Bar pregnvayl svaqf vg hfrshy sbe
                            gur zvffvba.>

Gur svefg cneg bs guvf rknzcyr vf {Dh'inQ yV'} <Vg vf hfrshy sbe gur
zvffvba> ({Dh'inQ} <sbe gur zvffvba,> {yV'} <vg vf hfrshy>). Gur frpbaq
cneg vf {arg gh'orw} <Bar pregnvayl svaqf gung> be <Bar pregnvayl
bofreirf gung.> Gur shyy pbafgehpgvba zvtug nyfb or genafyngrq
<Bar jvyy pregnvayl bofreir gung vg vf hfrshy gb gur zvffvba.> Abgr
gung nygubhtu gur jbeq <jvyy> znxrf n zber sybjvat genafyngvba,
gurer vf abguvat va gur Xyvatba fragrapr vaqvpngvat shgher
grafr.

  Jura gur ireo bs gur frpbaq fragrapr vf {arU} <jnag,> arvgure [[c.67]]
{'r'} abe {arg} vf hfrq, ohg gur pbafgehpgvba vf bgurejvfr vqragvpny
gb gung whfg qrfpevorq.

    {wVDbat iVarU} <V jnag gb fyrrc.>
    ({wVDbat} <V fyrrc,> {iVarU} <V jnag vg>)

    {dnyrtu iVarU} <V jnag gb frr lbh.>
    ({dnyrtu} <V frr lbh,> {iVarU} <V jnag vg>)

    {Qnyrtu iVarU} <V jnag lbh gb frr uvz/ure.>
    ({Qnyrtu} <lbh frr uvz/ure,> {iVarU} <V jnag vg>)

    {dnzn'ch' iVwbagn' iVarU} <V jnagrq gb pncgher cevfbaref.>

Va guvf svany rknzcyr, gur svefg cneg vf {dnzn'ch' iVwbagn'} <V
pncgherq cevfbaref> ({dnzn'ch'} <cevfbaref,> {iVwbagn'} <V pncgherq
gurz>). Abgr bapr ntnva gung gur nfcrpg znexre (va guvf pnfr,
{-gn'} <nppbzcyvfurq>) tbrf jvgu gur svefg ireo bayl; gur frpbaq
ireo, {iVarU} <V jnag vg,> vf arhgeny nf gb gvzr. Gur cnfg grafr bs
gur genafyngvba <(V jnagrq...)> pbzrf sebz gur nfcrpg znexre
ba gur svefg ireo.

  Fvzvyneyl, jvgu ireof bs fnlvat (<fnl, gryy, nfx,> rgp.), {'r'} naq
{arg} ner abg hfrq. Gur gjb cuenfrf fvzcyl sbyybj bar nabgure,
va rvgure beqre.

       {dnwn'ch' UVdntuDb'}
    be {UVdntuDb' dnwn'ch'} <V gbyq lbh abg gb vagreehcg zr.>

Guvf vf yvgrenyyl <V gbyq lbh, "Qba'g vagreehcg zr!"> be <"Qba'g
vagreehcg zr" V gbyq lbh> ({dnwn'ch'} <V gbyq lbh,> {UVdntuDb'} <qba'g
vagreehcg zr!>). Na nfcrpg znexre (urer, {-ch'} <cresrpgvir>) znl
nyjnlf or nggnpurq gb gur ireo bs fnlvat, ertneqyrff bs
jurgure vg vf gur svefg be frpbaq ireo.

  Svanyyl, gur hfr bs {eVagnU} gb vaqvpngr gung na npgvba vf
nppbzcyvfurq (frpgvba 4.2.7) vf nabgure rknzcyr bs gur gjb- [[xrrc ulcura]]
ireo (be gjb-fragrapr) pbafgehpgvba.


6.3. "Gb or"

Gurer vf ab ireo pbeerfcbaqvat gb Ratyvfu <gb or> va Xyvatba.
Ba gur bgure unaq, nyy cebabhaf (frpgvba 5.1) pna or hfrq nf
ireof, va gur frafr bs <V nz, lbh ner,> rgp.

    {gyuVatna wVU} <V nz n Xyvatba.> [[c.68]]
    {lnF FbU} <Lbh ner na bssvpre.>
    {chdch' punU} <Gurl ner puvyqera.>

  Gur cebabha nyjnlf sbyybjf gur abha.
  Fvzvyneyl, gurer vf ab ireo pbeerfcbaqvat gb <gb or> va gur
frafr bs "gb or ng n cynpr." Ntnva, gur cebabhaf ner hfrq,
sbyybjrq, jurer nccebcevngr, ol ireony fhssvkrf.

    {cn'jVwQnd wVUgnU} <V nz va zl dhnegref.>
                       ({cn'jVwQnd} <va zl ebbz,> {wVU} <V,>
                       {-gnU} <pbagvahbhf>)

  Va gur nobir rknzcyrf, gur fhowrpgf ner cebabhaf. Vs gur
fhowrpg vf n abha, vg sbyybjf gur guveq-crefba cebabha ({tunU}
<ur/fur,> {'bU} <vg,> {punU} <gurl,> {oVU} <gurl>) naq gnxrf gur {-'r'} <gbcvp>
fhssvk (frr frpgvba 3.3.5).

    {chdch' punU dnzn'ch' 'r'} <Gur cevfbaref ner puvyqera.> [[dnzn'ch' 'r':=dnzn'ch''r']]
    {cn'QnwQnd tunUgnU yn''r'} <Gur pbzznaqre vf va uvf
                               dhnegref.>

Gurfr fragraprf zvtug nyfb or genafyngrq <Nf sbe gur cevfbaref,
gurl ner puvyqera; Nf sbe gur pbzznaqre, ur vf va uvf dhnegref.>


6.4. Dhrfgvbaf

Gurer ner gjb glcrf bs dhrfgvbaf: gubfr juvpu znl or
nafjrerq "lrf" be "ab," naq gubfr juvpu erdhver rkcynan-
gvbaf nf nafjref.
  Lrf/ab dhrfgvbaf ner sbezrq jvgu gur Glcr 9 fhssvk {-'n'}
nqqrq gb gur ireo. Rknzcyrf ner tvira va frpgvba 4.2.9.
  Nccebcevngr nafjref gb lrf/ab dhrfgvbaf ner:

    {UVwn'} be {UVFynU} <lrf>
    {tubor'} <ab>

  Gur bgure glcr bs dhrfgvba pbagnvaf n dhrfgvba jbeq:

    {punl'} <ubj?>
    {tubetu} <jura?>
    {ahd} <jung?>
    {ahdQnd} <jurer?> [[c.69]]
    {dngyu} <jul?>
    {'ne} <ubj znal? ubj zhpu?>
    {'Vi} <jub?>

  Sbe {'Vi} <jub?> naq {ahd} <jung?> gur dhrfgvba jbeq svgf vagb gur
fragrapr va gur cbfvgvba gung jbhyq or bpphcvrq ol gur
nafjre. Sbe rknzcyr:

    {lnF yrtu 'Vi} <Jub frrf gur bssvpre?>
    {'Vi yrtu lnF} <Jubz qbrf gur bssvpre frr?>

Va gur svefg dhrfgvba, vg vf gur fhowrpg juvpu vf orvat nfxrq
nobhg, fb {'Vi} <jub?> tbrf va gur fhowrpg cbfvgvba, sbyybjvat gur
ireo {yrtu} <ur/fur frrf uvz/ure.> Va gur frpbaq pnfr, gur bowrpg vf
orvat dhrfgvbarq, fb gur dhrfgvba jbeq tbrf va gur bowrpg [[dhrfgvbarq:=nfxrq sbe]]
cbfvgvba, orsber gur ireo.
  Fvzvyneyl jvgu {ahd} <jung?:>

    {Qhw tubFgnU ahd} <Jung vf pbzvat gbjneq gur fuvc?>
                      ({Qhw} <fuvc, irffry,> {tubFgnU} <vg vf
                      cebprrqvat gbjneq vg>)
    {ahd yrtu lnF} <Jung qbrf gur bssvpre frr?>

  Obgu {'Vi} naq {ahd} ner gerngrq nf abhaf nf sne nf gur
cebabzvany cersvkrf ner pbaprearq. Gung vf, gurl ner pbafvq-
rerq guveq crefba.

    {ahtubFgnU ahd} <Jung vf pbzvat gbjneq hf?> ({ahtubFgnU} <vg
                  vf cebprrqvat gbjneq hf>)
    {ahd Qnyrtu} <Jung qb lbh frr?> ({Qnyrtu} <lbh frr vg>)

  Gur jbeq sbe <jurer?,> {ahdQnd,} vf npghnyyl {ahd} <jung?>
sbyybjrq ol gur fhssvk {-Qnd} <ybpngvir> (frr frpgvba 3.3.5). Nf
jbhyq nal ybpngvir cuenfr (frr frpgvba 6.1), vg pbzrf ng gur
ortvaavat bs gur fragrapr.

    {ahdQnd Fb'gnU lnF} <Jurer vf gur bssvpre uvqvat?>
                        ({Fb'gnU} <ur/fur vf uvqvat>)

  Guerr bgure dhrfgvba jbeqf yvxrjvfr bpphe ng gur ortvaavat
bs gur fragrapr. [[c.70]]

    {tubetu Unj'ch' lnF} <Jura qvq gur bssvpre syrr?>
                         ({Unj'ch'} <ur/fur unf syrq>)
    {dngyu Unj'ch' lnF} <Jul qvq gur bssvpre syrr?>
    {punl' Unj'ch' lnF} <Ubj qvq gur bssvpre syrr?>

  Abgr nyfb:

    {punl' when'} <Jung ner lbhe beqref?>

Guvf vf npghnyyl {punl'} <ubj?,> {when'} <lbh pbzznaq hf;> guhf,
<Ubj qb lbh pbzznaq hf?>
  Gur dhrfgvba jbeq {punl'} <ubj?> znl or hfrq nf n bar-jbeq
fragrapr zrnavat <Ubj qvq guvf unccra? Jung unccrarq?
Jung gur---?>
  Svanyyl, {'ne} <ubj znal? ubj zhpu?> sbyybjf gur abha gb
juvpu vg ersref. Vg pna arire sbyybj n abha jvgu n cyheny fhssvk
({-ch', -zrl, -Qh';} frr frpgvba 3.3.2).

    {Unj'ch' lnF 'ne} <Ubj znal bssvpref syrq?>
                      ({Unj'ch'} <gurl syrq,> {lnF} <bssvpre>)
    {aVa 'ne jVtunw} <Ubj zhpu shry qb jr unir?>
                     ({aVa} <shry,> {jVtunw} <jr unir vg>)


6.5. Pbzznaqf

Pbzznaqf ner tvira jvgu nccebcevngr vzcrengvir cersvkrf.
Frr frpgvbaf 4.1.2, 4.3.


6.6. Pbzcnengvirf naq fhcreyngvirf

Gur vqrn bs fbzrguvat orvat zber be terngre guna fbzrguvat
ryfr (pbzcnengvir) vf rkcerffrq ol zrnaf bs n pbafgehpgvba
juvpu pna or ercerfragrq ol gur sbyybjvat sbezhyn:

  N D {ynj'} O D {chF}

Va guvf sbezhyn, N naq O ner gur gjb guvatf orvat pbzcnerq
naq D vf gur dhnyvgl juvpu vf orvat zrnfherq. Gur gjb
Xyvatba jbeqf va gur sbezhyn ner {ynj'} <or znal> naq {chF} <or
srj.> Guhf, vg fnlf <N'f D vf znal, O'f D vf srj> be <N unf zber D
guna O unf> be <N vf D-re guna O.>
  Nal ireo rkcerffvat n dhnyvgl be pbaqvgvba znl svg vagb gur
D fybg. [[c.71]]

    {yn' wnd ynj' lnF wnd chF} <Gur pbzznaqre vf obyqre guna
                               gur bssvpre.>
                               ({yn'} <pbzznaqre,> {wnd} <or obyq,> {lnF}
                               <bssvpre>)

  Gb rkcerff gur fhcreyngvir, gung fbzrguvat vf gur zbfg be
gur terngrfg bs nyy, gur abha {Ubpu} <nyy> vf hfrq va gur O cbfvgvba:

    {yn' wnd ynj' Ubpu wnd chF} <Gur pbzznaqre vf obyqrfg
                                bs nyy.>

Va pbzcnengvir naq fhcreyngvir pbafgehpgvbaf, gur ireo bs
dhnyvgl ({wnd} <or obyq> va gur fragraprf nobir) zhfg or fnvq
gjvpr. [[c.72]]


7. PYVCCRQ XYVATBA

Gur cerprqvat tenzzngvpny fxrgpu qrfpevorf "cebcre"
Xyvatba, gung vf, Xyvatba nf vg vf gnhtug va Xyvatba fpubbyf be
gb aba-Xyvatbaf. Va npghny qnl-gb-qnl hfr, ubjrire, fcbxra
Xyvatba znl inel fbzrjung sebz vgf "cebcre" sbez, hfhnyyl
ol yrnivat fbzr ryrzragf bhg. Guvf nooerivngrq sbez bs
fcrnxvat, pnyyrq Pyvccrq Xyvatba ol Xyvatba tenzznevnaf, vf
urneq dhvgr serdhragyl va zvyvgnel pbagrkgf jurer dhvpx
---engure guna rybdhrag---pbzzhavpngvba vf qrrzrq n iveghr.
Cebonoyl sbe fvzvyne ernfbaf, Pyvccrq Xyvatba vf hfrq dhvgr
rkgrafviryl va nyy jnyxf bs Xyvatba yvsr.
  Fbzr bs gur srngherf bs Pyvccrq Xyvatba ner qrfpevorq
orybj.


7.1. Pbzznaqf

Va tvivat pbzznaqf, gur vzcrengvir cersvk (frpgvba 4.1.2)
znl or yrsg bss, yrnivat gur oner ireo.

    Cebcre Xyvatba: {lVonU} <Sver (gur gbecrqbrf)!>
    Pyvccrq Xyvatba: {onU}

    Cebcre Xyvatba: {jVl lVpun'} <Fubj gur gnpgvpny qvfcynl!>
    Pyvccrq Xyvatba: {jVl pun'}
      ({jVl} <gnpgvpny qvfcynl ba zbavgbe,> {pun'} <fubj, cebwrpg>)

    Cebcre Xyvatba: {Ur puh' lVtubF} <Sbyybj n arj pbhefr!> [[c.73]]
    Pyvccrq Xyvatba: {Ur puh' tubF}
      ({Ur} <pbhefr,> {puh'} <or arj,> {tubF} <sbyybj n pbhefr>)

  Jura gur bowrpg abha vf pevgvpny, naq jung vf gb or qbar
jvgu gung abha vf boivbhf (be fubhyq or boivbhf) gb gur
yvfgrare, gung abha vgfrys znl freir nf gur pbzznaq.

    Cebcre Xyvatba: {puhlQnU lVynD} <Sver gur guehfgref!>
    Pyvccrq Xyvatba: {puhlQnU} <Guehfgref!>
      ({puhlQnU} <guehfgref,> {ynD} <sver, raretvmr>)

    Cebcre Xyvatba: {UnFgn lVpun'} <Fubj gur ivfhny qvfcynl!>
    Pyvccrq Xyvatba: {UnFgn} <Ivfhny (qvfcynl)!>
      ({UnFgn} <ivfhny qvfcynl ba zbavgbe,> {pun'} <fubj,
      cebwrpg>)

  Svanyyl, bgure tenzzngvpny znexref, cnegvphyneyl abha fhs-
svkrf, znl or yrsg bhg bs pbzznaqf.

    Cebcre Xyvatba: {wbycn'Qnd lVwnU} <Tb gb gur genafcbeg ebbz!>
    Pyvccrq Xyvatba: {wbycn' lVwnU}
      ({wbycn'} <genafcbeg ebbz,> {-Qnd} <ybpngvir,> {wnU} <tb>)

  Vg vf abg pbzzba, jura abha fhssvkrf ner pubccrq, sbe gur
vzcrengvir cersvk ba gur ireo gb or qebccrq nf jryy.


7.2. Erfcbafrf gb pbzznaqf, fgnghf ercbegf

Erfcbafrf gb pbzznaqf naq fgnghf ercbegf ner nyfb cebar gb
pyvccvat.

    Cebcre Xyvatba: {Fb'jV' iVpuh'gn'} <V unir ratntrq gur pybnx-
                    vat qrivpr.>
    Cebcre Xyvatba: {Fb'jV' puh'yh'gn'} <Gur pybnxvat qrivpr
                    unf orra ratntrq.>
    Pyvccrq Xyvatba: {Fb'jV' puh'gn'} <Pybnxvat qrivpr ratntrq.>
      ({Fb'jV'} <pybnxvat qrivpr,> {iVpuh'gn'} <V unir ratntrq vg,>
      {puh'yh'gn'} <vg unf orra ratntrq>)

  Va gur cerprqvat rknzcyr, gur pyvccrq sbez pna pbeerfcbaq
gb rvgure n qebccvat bs gur cersvk {iV-} <V--vg> be gur fhssvk {-yh'}
<vaqrsvavgr fhowrpg.>

    Cebcre Xyvatba: {wVlnwpuh'} <V haqrefgnaq pyrneyl.>
    Pyvccrq Xyvatba: {lnwpuh'} <Haqrefgbbq pyrneyl.>
      ({lnw} <haqrefgnaq,> {-puh'} <pyrneyl, cresrpgyl>) [[c.74]]

  Va guvf svany rknzcyr, gur pyvccrq sbez, ynpxvat gur cebabz-
vany cersvk {wV-} <V,> vf n yvxryl erfcbafr gb n dhrfgvba va pyvccrq
sbez, fhpu nf {lnw'n'} <Haqrefgbbq?> (pbzcner Cebcre Xyvatba
{oVlnw'n'} <Qb lbh haqrefgnaq?>).


7.3. Qherff, rkpvgrzrag

Jura va n fvghngvba bs terng qnatre be jura vzzrqvngr npgvba
znl or arprffnel, n Xyvatba vf ncg gb qebc cebabzvany
cersvkrf. Guvf pyvccrq sbez vf nyfb pbzzba jura n Xyvatba vf
rkpvgrq sbe fbzr ernfba.

    Cebcre Xyvatba: {dnzn'ch' iVwbagn' iVarU} <V jnagrq gb
                    pncgher cevfbaref.>
    Pyvccrq Xyvatba: {dnzn'ch' wbagn' arU} <Jnagrq cevfbaref!>
      ({dnzn'ch'} <cevfbaref,> {iVwbagn'} <V pncgherq gurz,> {iVarU} <V
      jnag gurz>)

  Va pbagrkg, vg jbhyq or pyrne gung gur fcrnxre vf gur bar
qbvat gur jnagvat (naq pncghevat), rira gubhtu gur cebabzv-
any cersvk {iV-} <V--gurz> vf zvffvat. [[c.75]]

VAGEBQHPGBEL ERZNEXF

Guvf qvpgvbanel pbagnvaf sbhe cnegf: (1) Xyvatba gb Ratyvfu,
(2) Ratyvfu gb Xyvatba, (3) yvfg bs nssvkrf va Xyvatba nycun-
orgvpny beqre, (4) yvfg bs nssvkrf va Ratyvfu nycunorgvpny
beqre.
  Xyvatba nycunorgvpny beqre vf nf sbyybjf:

    {n, o, pu, Q, r, tu, U, V, w, y, z, a, at,
    b, c, d, D, e, F, g, gyu, h, i, j, l, '}

Abgr gung {pu, tu, at,} naq {gyu} ner pbafvqrerq frcnengr yrggref.
Guhf gur flyynoyr {ab} jbhyq cerprqr gur flyynoyr {atn} va gur
Xyvatba yvfg.
  Rnpu Xyvatba jbeq vf gnttrq nf gb glcr (abha, ireo, rgp.).
Guvf gnt bpphef ng gur raq bs gur Ratyvfu genafyngvba. Gur
nooerivngvbaf hfrq gb vaqvpngr jbeq glcrf ner:

    nqi   nqireovny      (frpgvba 5.4)
    pbaw  pbawhapgvba    (frpgvba 5.3)
    rkpy  rkpynzngvba    (frpgvba 5.5)
    a     abha           (frpgvba 3)
    ahz   ahzore         (frpgvba 5.2)
    ceb   cebabha        (frpgvba 5.1)
    dhrf  dhrfgvba jbeq  (frpgvba 6.4)
    i     ireo           (frpgvba 4) [[c.78]]

  Va ybbxvat guebhtu gur qvpgvbanel, vg jvyy or abgvprq gung
gurer ner n ahzore bs abha/ireo cnvef; gung vf, gur fnzr jbeq
vf obgu n abha naq n ireo. Shgurezber, gurer ner fbzr jbeqf [[Shgurezber:=Shegurezber]]
juvpu ner vqragvpny va sbez (naq arneyl vqragvpny va zrnavat)
gb fbzr fhssvkrf (sbe rknzcyr, {ynU} vf n abha zrnavat <nppbz-
cyvfuzrag> naq {-ynU} vf n ireo fhssvk zrnavat <pna, noyr>).
  Gurer ner nyfb n ahzore bs Xyvatba flabalzf; gung vf gjb
Xyvatba jbeqf jvgu vqragvpny zrnavatf (sbe rknzcyr, {wbu, wnj} [[wbu:=wbU]]
<ybeq,> {purgiV', QhF} <gbecrqb ghor>). Bppnfvbanyyl bar zrzore bs
fhpu n flabalz frg pna or nanylmrq. Guhf, {onUjV'} <thaare>
pbafvfgf bs gur ireo {onU} <sver (n gbecrqb)> cyhf gur fhssvk {-jV'}
<bar jub qbrf fbzrguvat.> Gur bgure jbeq sbe <thaare,> {zngun',} [[zngun':=zngUn']]
erznvaf vzcreivbhf gb nanylfvf. Fbzrgvzrf bar zrzore bs n
frg znl or cnegvnyyl nanylmrq. Sbe rknzcyr, {wbagn'} <ratvar>
ortvaf jvgu {wba,} juvpu vf nyfb sbhaq va {wbajV'} <ratvarre,> naq
raqf jvgu {gn',} juvpu nyfb bpphef va {zVdgn'} <znpuvarel.> Gur
bgure zrzoref bs gurfr flabalz frgf, {DhD} <ratvar> naq {wb'}
<znpuvarel,> pnaabag or shegure nanylmrq. (Vg vf yvxryl gung [[pnaabag:=pnaabg]]
gurer ner frgf bs flabalzf jvgu guerr be zber zrzoref, ohg
abar unf orra sbhaq gb qngr.)
  Vg unf abg lrg orra cbffvoyr gb qrgrezvar ubj, be jurgure,
gur flabalzf ner hfrq qvssreragvnyyl. Creuncf gurer vf n
fhttrfgvba bs Xyvatba fbpvny fgehpgher uvqqra urer, sbe znal
bs gur flabalz frgf ner jbeqf eryngvat gb zvyvgnel be tbirea-
zragny enax (fhpu nf {lnF, 'hgyu} <bssvpre>). Ba gur bgure unaq,
fbzr bs gur cnvevatf ner jbeqf ersreevat gb zrpunavpf be
ratvarrevat (fhpu nf <ratvar> naq <gbecrqb ghor,> nf vyyhfgengrq
nobir). Creuncf n zber gubebhtu haqrefgnaqvat bs Xyvatba
grpuabybtl jbhyq erirny gung gurer vf vaqrrq n qvssrerapr va
zrnavat nzbat zrzoref bs rnpu frg. Qrfcvgr gur pheerag
vapbzcyrgr haqrefgnaqvat bs flabalzf, gur fghqrag bs
Xyvatba pna or eryngviryl nffherq gung ab znwbe fbpvny oyhaqre
jvyy or pbzzvggrq ol pubbfvat bar engure guna gur bgure
zrzore bs n flabalz frg.
  Gurfr inevbhf cnvevatf (abha/ireo, jbeq/fhssvk, flabalz
frgf) ner bs terng uvfgbevpny vagrerfg, sbe gurl fheryl vaqvpngr
fbzrguvat nobhg rneyvre fgntrf bs gur ynathntr. Hasbeghangr-
yl, n yvathvfgvp uvfgbel bs Xyvatba vf orlbaq gur fpbcr bs gur
cerfrag jbex.
  Sbe rnfr bs ersrerapr, Ratyvfu ragevrf va gur Ratyvfu- [[xrrc ulcura]] [[c.79]]
Xyvatba frpgvba bs guvf qvpgvbanel ortva jvgu gur jbeq gung gur
hfre jbhyq zbfg yvxryl or ybbxvat sbe, rira gubhtu guvf znl ng
gvzrf or tenzzngvpnyyl vapbeerpg. Guvf svefg jbeq vf, jura
nccebcevngr, sbyybjrq ol gur pbeerpg genafyngvba. Sbe rknz-
cyr, Ratyvfu nqwrpgvirf (r.t., <obyq>) pbeerfcbaq gb Xyvatba
ireof, zbfg npphengryl genafyngrq hfvat gur Ratyvfu ireo <gb or>
(r.t., <or obyq>). Nyy fhpu jbeqf ner ragrerq jvgu gur nqwrpgvir
svefg, sbyybjrq ol gur npphengr genafyngvba (r.t., <obyq, or
obyq>). Fvzvyneyl, jura n Xyvatba jbeq vf genafyngrq vagb na
Ratyvfu cuenfr (r.t., <unir n urnqnpur>), gur svefg jbeq va gur
Ratyvfu ragel vf gur xrl jbeq va gur cuenfr, sbyybjrq ol gur
cebcre genafyngvba (r.t., <urnqnpur, unir n urnqnpur>). [[c.80]]

VAGEBQHPGVBA GB GUR
NQQRAQHZ

Gur bevtvany rqvgvba bs guvf qvpgvbanel jnf arire vagraqrq gb
pbagnva n pbzcyrgr qrfpevcgvba bs gur Xyvatba ynathntr, ohg
bayl na bhgyvar bs fbzr bs vgf zber vzcbegnag tenzzngvpny
srngherf naq n ercerfragngvir fnzcyr bs vgf ibpnohynel. Fvapr
vgf nccrnenapr, fghql bs gur ynathntr unf pbagvahrq naq n
terng qrny zber unf orra yrnearq. Hasbeghangryl, qhr gb n
ahzore bs snpgbef, vapyhqvat gur erprffvba pheeragyl nssrpg-
vat zbfg bs guvf frpgbe nf jryy nf erprag cbyvgvpny punatrf,
erfrnepu shaqf unir orpbzr zber qvssvphyg gb pbzr ol,
qrynlvat gur pbzcyrgvba bs nanylfvf bs gur ynathntr. Vaqrrq,
jbex unf orra fgnyyrq ba n ahzore bs jbegujuvyr cebwrpgf,
vapyhqvat gur <Xyvatba Raplpybcrqvn> naq gur <Ebzhyna
Puerfgbzngul.> Arireguryrff, rabhtu arj vasbezngvba unf
orra tyrnarq nobhg Xyvatba gung nqqvat na nqqraqhz gb
gur qvpgvbanel, rira n oevrs bar, frrzf orarsvpvny.

  Va guvf nqqraqhz, gur frpgvba-ahzorevat flfgrz hfrq va
gur znva obql bs gur qvpgvbanel vf rzcyblrq fb gung pebff
ersreraprf znl or rnfvyl znqr.

  Bapr ntnva, gur nhgube jbhyq yvxr gb gunax gur Srqrengvba
Fpvragvsvp Erfrnepu Pbhapvy sbe vgf fhccbeg bs guvf cebwrpg,
naq, zber vzcbegnagyl, jbhyq yvxr gb tvir perqvg gb gubfr
jub ernyyl znxr guvf rssbeg cbffvoyr: gur vapernfvat ahzore
bs Xyvatbaf jub ner rntre gb funer gurve ynathntr naq
phygher jvgu gur erfg bs hf. {gnUwnw obd.} [[c.174]]


3. ABHAF

3.3.1. Glcr 1: Abha Fhssvkrf: Nhtzragngvir/qvzvahgvir

{-bl} <raqrnezrag>

  Guvf vf na vaserdhragyl hfrq, ohg abarguryrff irel vagre-
rfgvat abha fhssvk. Vg vf n irel crphyvne fhssvk orpnhfr vg vf gur
bayl fhssvk gung ortvaf jvgu n ibjry engure guna n pbafbanag.
(Gubhtu gurer ner ab rknzcyrf, vg vf fhfcrpgrq gung sbe gubfr
srj abhaf juvpu raq va n ibjry, {'} vf vafregrq orsber guvf
fhssvk.) Gur fhssvk hfhnyyl sbyybjf n abha ersreevat gb n
eryngvir (<zbgure, sngure,> rgp.), ohg vg pbhyq nyfb sbyybj n abha
sbe na navzny, rfcrpvnyyl n crg, naq zrnaf gung gur fcrnxre vf
cnegvphyneyl sbaq bs jungrire gur abha ersref gb. Vg vf
fgebatyl fhttrfgrq gung aba-angvir fcrnxref bs Xyvatba
nibvq guvf fhssvk hayrff gurl xabj jung gurl ner trggvat vagb.

avat bs fragraprf gheaf bhg gb or abg dhvgr npphengr. Sbe n
zber pbeerpg qrfpevcgvba, frr Frpgvba 6.7. [[Frpgvba:=frpgvba]]
  Gurer vf n frpbaq jbeq (va nqqvgvba gb {arU} <bayl, zreryl>)
juvpu svgf vagb guvf pngrtbel qrfcvgr vgf irel crphyvne oruni-

    {wnl'} <vagrafryl>

5.5 Rkpynzngvbaf [[5.5:=5.5.]]

Nf vg gheaf bhg, phefvat vf n bar neg nzbat Xyvatbaf. Gurer
ner znal zber phefrf guna gubfr guerr yvfgrq va gur rneyvre
rqvgvba bs gur qvpgvbanel. Vg vf abg nyjnlf pyrne ubj gb hfr
gur phefrf, ohg fbzr ner pregnvayl rcvgurgvpny (hfrq sbe
anzr-pnyyvat), juvyr bguref frrz gb unir n zber trareny
nccyvpngvba. N srj nqqvgvbany phefrf ner yvfgrq orybj.

    {Dbicngyu}

6. FLAGNK


6.4. Dhrfgvbaf

Gnt dhrfgvbaf (raqvat n fgngrzrag jvgu n dhrfgvba fhpu nf
"evtug?" be "vfa'g gung fb?") ner sbezrq ol hfvat gur ireo {tne} [[tne:=dne]]
<or npphengr> cyhf gur fhssvk {-'n'} <vagreebtngvir.> Guvf jbeq rvgure
sbyybjf gur ireo be ryfr pbzrf ng gur raq bs gur fragrapr.

                         {UbQ} <pncgnva>)


6.7. Cynprzrag bs nqireovny ryrzragf

Vg jnf rneyvre gubhtug gung nyy nqireovnyf (rkprcg {arU} <bayl>)
pbzr ng gur ortvaavat bs gur fragrapr. Guvf vf serdhragyl gur
pnfr, ohg jung vf ernyyl tbvat ba vf gung gur nqireovny
cerprqrf gur bowrpg-ireo-abha pbafgehpgvba. Vg vf cbffvoyr [[bowrpg-ireo-abha:=bowrpg-ireo-fhowrpg]]
sbe na ryrzrag bs nabgure glcr gb cerprqr gur nqireo. Zbfg
pbzzbayl, guvf vf n gvzr ryrzrag (n abha be cuenfr zrnavat
<gbqnl, ng fvk b'pybpx,> rgp.).

    {QnUwnw abz Fbcch'} <Gbqnl gurl ngr dhvpxyl> ({QnUwnw}
                        <gbqnl,> {abz} <dhvpxyl,> {Fbcch'} <gurl>
                        <ngr>) [[c.180]]

  Gur nqireovny znl npghnyyl sbyybj gur bowrpg abha (ohg
fgvyy cerprqr gur ireo) jura gur bowrpg abha vf gbcvpnyvmrq ol
zrnaf bs gur abha fhssvk {-'r'} (frr Frpgvba 3.3.5.). [[Frpgvba:=frpgvba]]

    {UndjV' 'r' QnU lVFnz} <Svaq gur FHETRBA abj!> [[UndjV' 'r':=UndjV''r']]
                           ({UndjV'} <fhetrba,> {QnU} <abj,>
                           {lVFnz} <svaq uvz/ure!>)


6.8. Vaqverpg bowrpgf

Juvyr gur bowrpg bs gur ireo vf gur erpvcvrag bs gur npgvba, gur
vaqverpg bowrpg znl or pbafvqrerq gur orarsvpvnel. Va n
Xyvatba fragrapr, gur vaqverpg bowrpg cerprqrf gur bowrpg
naq vf fhssvkrq jvgu gur Glcr 5 abha fhssvk {-inQ} <sbe, vagraqrq
sbe.> Gur fhssvk znl or nggnpurq gb rvgure n abha be n
cebabha.

    {lnFinQ gnw aboch' dnzn'} <Gur cevfbare tnir gur bssvpre>
                              <gur xavsr> ({lnF} <bssvpre,> {gnw}
                              <xavsr,> {aboch'} <tnir,> {dnzn'}
                              <cevfbare>)

                          <oevat,> {lnF} <bssvpre>) [[c.181]]
